  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Shirao K, et al. J Clin Oncol 1997;15:921–927.

2.14.2.8 IPB

  • Irinotecan: 65 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Cisplatin: 30 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Bevacizumab: 15 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Shah MA, et al. J Clin Oncol 2006;24:5201–5206.

2.14.2.9 Docetaxel + Cisplatin

  • Docetaxel: 85 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cisplatin: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Ajani JA, et al. Proc Am Soc Clin Oncol 2000;20:165a (abstract 657).

2.14.2.10 IDO

  • Irinotecan: 150 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Docetaxel: 60 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Oxaliplatin: 85 mg/m2 IV on day 2
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Di Lauro L, et al. Br J Cancer 2007;97:593–599.

2.14.2.11 Capecitabine + Cisplatin

  • Capecitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 PO bid on days 1–14
  • Cisplatin: 80 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Kang Y, et al. J Clin Oncol 2006;24:18S (LBA4018).

2.14.2.12 XP + Trastuzumab

  • Capecitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 PO bid on days 1–14
  • Cisplatin: 80 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Trastuzumab: 8 mg/kg IV loading dose, then 6 mg/kg IV every 3 weeks
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days [280].

2.14.2.13 FP + Trastuzumab

  • 5-Fluorouracil: 800 mg/m2 IV continuous infusion on days 1–5
  • Cisplatin: 80 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Trastuzumab: 8 mg/kg IV loading dose, then 6 mg/kg IV every 3 weeks
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

van Cutsem EV, et al. J Clin Oncol 2009;27:18s (LBA4509).

2.14.2.14 FLO

  • 5-Fluorouracil: 2,600 mg/m2 IV on day 1 as a continuous infusion over 24 hours
  • Leucovorin: 200 mg/m2 IV on day 1 as a 2-hour infusion
  • Oxaliplatin: 85 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 14 days.

Al-Batran SE, et al. J Clin Oncol 2008;26:1435–1442.

2.14.2.15 mFOLFOX6

  • Oxaliplatin: 100 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • 5-Fluorouracil: 2,400 mg/m2 IV infusion for 46 hours starting on day 1
  • Leucovorin: 100 mg/m2 IV on day 1 as a 2-hour infusion prior to 5-FU
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks.

Keam B, et al. BMC Cancer 2008;8:148.

2.14.2.16 Paclitaxel + Ramucirumab

  • Paclitaxel: 80 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Ramucirumab: 8 mg/kg IV on days 1 and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Wilke H, et al. Lancet Oncol 2014;11;1224–1235.

2.14.3 Metastatic Disease - Single-Agent Regimens

2.14.3.1 5-Fluorouracil

  • 5-Fluorouracil: 500 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Cullinan SA, et al. J Clin Oncol 1994;12:412–416.

2.14.3.2 5-Fluorouracil + Leucovorin

  • 5-Fluorouracil: 370 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Leucovorin: 200 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Cascinu S, et al. J Chemother 1992;4:185–188.

2.14.3.3 Docetaxel

  • Docetaxel: 100 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

O’Connell MJ. J Clin Oncol 1985;3:1032–1039.

or - Docetaxel: 36 mg/m2 IV weekly for 6 weeks - Repeat cycle every 8 weeks.

Ajani JA. Oncology 2002;16 (suppl 6):89–96.

2.14.3.4 Ramucirumab

  • Ramucirumab: 8 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 14 days.

Fuchs CS, et al. Lancet 2014;383:31–39.

2.14.3.5 Pembrolizumab

  • Pembrolizumab: 200 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 3 weeks.

Fuchs CS, et al. JAMA Oncol 2018;4:e180013.

2.15 GASTROINTESTINAL STROMAL TUMOR (GIST)

2.15.1 Adjuvant Therapy

2.15.1.1 Imatinib

  • Imatinib: 400 mg/day PO
  • Continue treatment for a total of 3 years.

Joensu H, et al. J Clin Oncol 2011;29:18S (LBA1).

2.15.2 Metastatic Disease - Single-Agent Regimens

2.15.2.1 Imatinib

  • Imatinib: 400 mg/day PO
  • Continue treatment until disease progression. May increase dose to 600 mg/day if no response is seen. In patients with KIT exon 9 (or exon 11) mutation, use dose of 800 mg/day (400 mg bid).

Demetri GD, et al. N Engl J Med 2002;347:472–480.

2.15.2.2 Nilotinib

  • Nilotinib: 400 mg PO bid
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Montemurro M, et al. Eur J Cancer 2009;45:2293–2297.

2.15.2.3 Sunitinib

  • Sunitinib: 50 mg/day PO for 4 weeks
  • Repeat cycle every 6 weeks.

Demetri GD, et al. Proc GI ASCO 2006 (abstract 8).

2.15.2.4 Sorafenib

  • Sorafenib: 400 mg/day PO bid
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Italiano A, et al. Ann Surg Oncol 2012;19:1551–1559.

2.15.2.5 Regorafenib

  • Regorafenib: 160 mg/day PO for 21 days
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Demetri GD, et al. Lancet 2013;381:295–302.

2.16 HEAD AND NECK CANCER

2.16.1 Combined Modality Therapy

2.16.1.1 Cetuximab + Radiation Therapy

  • Cetuximab: 400 mg/m2 IV loading dose, 1 week before radiation therapy, then 250 mg/m2 IV weekly
  • Radiation therapy: 200 cGy/day for 5 days per week (total dose, 7,000 cGy)
  • Cetuximab is given concurrently with radiation therapy.

Bonner JA, et al. N Engl J Med 2006;354:567–578.

2.16.1.2 TPF Induction Chemotherapy Followed by Carboplatin + Radiation Therapy

  • Docetaxel: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cisplatin: 75–100 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • 5-Fluorouracil: 1,000 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Repeat cycle every 3 weeks for 3 cycles followed by:
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 1.5, IV weekly for 7 weeks during radiation therapy
  • Radiation therapy: 200 cGy/day to a total dose of 7,400 cGy
  • At the completion of chemoradiotherapy, surgical resection as indicated.

Posner MR, et al. N Engl J Med 2007;357:1705–1715.

2.16.2 Combination Regimens

2.16.2.1 TIP

  • Paclitaxel: 175 mg/m2 IV over 3 hours on day 1
  • Mesna: 400 mg/m2 IV before ifosfamide and 200 mg/m2 IV, 4 hours after ifosfamide
  • Cisplatin: 60 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21–28 days.

Shin DS, et al. J Clin Oncol 1998;16:1325–1330.

2.16.2.2 TPF

  • Docetaxel: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cisplatin: 75–100 mg/m2 IV over 24 hours on day 1
  • 5-Fluorouracil: 1,000 mg/m2 over 24 hours on days 1–4
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Posner M, et al. J Clin Oncol 2001;19:1096–1104.

2.16.2.3 TIC

  • Paclitaxel: 175 mg/m2 IV over 3 hours on day 1
  • Ifosfamide: 1,000 mg/m2 IV over 2 hours on days 1–3
  • Mesna: 400 mg/m2 IV before ifosfamide and 200 mg/m2 IV, 4 hours after ifosfamide
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21–28 days.

Shin DM, et al. Cancer 1999;91:1316–1323.

2.16.2.4 Paclitaxel + Carboplatin

  • Paclitaxel: 175 mg/m2 IV over 3 hours on day 1
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Fountzilas G, et al. Semin Oncol 1997;24 (Suppl 2):65–67.

2.16.2.5 Paclitaxel + Cisplatin

  • Paclitaxel: 175 mg/m2 IV over 3 hours on day 1
  • Cisplatin: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 2
  • G-CSF: 5 µg/kg/day SC on days 4–10
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Hitt R, et al. Semin Oncol 1995;22 (Suppl 15):50–54.

2.16.2.6 PF

  • Cisplatin: 100 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • 5-Fluorouracil: 1,000 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21–28 days.

Kish JA, et al. Cancer 1984;53:1819–1824.

2.16.2.7 Carboplatin + 5-FU

  • Carboplatin: AUC of 5, IV on day 1
  • 5-Fluorouracil: 1,000 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Vokes EE, et al. Cancer 1989;63 (Suppl 6):1048–1053.

2.16.2.8 PF + Cetuximab

  • Cisplatin: 100 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • 5-Fluorouracil: 1,000 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Cetuximab: 400 mg/m2 IV loading dose, then 250 mg/m2 IV weekly
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for up to 6 cycles. If no evidence of disease progression at the end of 6 cycles, can continue with weekly cetuximab.

Vermorken JB, et al. N Engl J Med 2008;359:1116–1127.

2.16.2.9 Carboplatin + 5-FU 1 Cetuximab

  • Carboplatin: AUC of 5, IV on day 1
  • 5-Fluorouracil: 1,000 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Cetuximab: 400 mg/m2 IV loading dose, then 250 mg/m2 IV weekly
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for up to 6 cycles. If no evidence of disease progression at the end of 6 cycles, can continue with weekly cetuximab.

Vermorken JB, et al. N Engl J Med 2008;359:1116–1127.

2.16.2.10 Cisplatin + Cetuximab

  • Cisplatin: 100 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cetuximab: 400 mg/m2 IV loading dose, then 250 mg/m2 IV weekly
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Burtness B, et al. J Clin Oncol 2005;23:8646–8654.

2.16.2.11 PF-Larynx Preservation

  • Cisplatin: 100 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • 5-Fluorouracil: 1,000 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–5
  • Radiation therapy: 6,600–7,600 cGy in 180–200 cGy fractions
  • Repeat cycle every 21–28 days for 3 cycles.

Veterans Affairs Laryngeal Cancer Study Group. N Engl J Med 1991;324:1685–1690.

2.16.2.12 Concurrent Chemoradiation Therapy for Laryngeal Preservation

  • Cisplatin: 100 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 22, and 43
  • Radiation therapy: 7,000 cGy in 200 cGy fractions
  • Administer cisplatin concurrently with radiation therapy.

Forastiere AA, et al. N Engl J Med 2003;349:2091–2098.

2.16.2.13 Chemoradiotherapy for Nasopharyngeal Cancer

  • Cisplatin: 100 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 22, and 43 during radiotherapy
  • Radiation therapy: Total dose of 7,000 cGy in 180–200 cGy fractions
  • At the completion of chemoradiotherapy, chemotherapy is administered as follows:
  • Cisplatin: 80 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • 5-Fluorouracil: 1,000 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for a total of 3 cycles.

Al-Sarraf M, et al. J Clin Oncol 1998;16:1310–1317.

2.16.2.14 VP

  • Vinorelbine: 25 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Cisplatin: 80 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Gebbia V, et al. Am J Clin Oncol 1995;18:293–296.

2.16.3 Single-Agent Regimens

2.16.3.1 Docetaxel

  • Docetaxel: 100 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Dreyfuss A, et al. Proc Am Soc Clin Oncol 1995;14:875a.

2.16.3.2 Paclitaxel

  • Paclitaxel: 250 mg/m2 IV over 24 hours on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days. or
  • Paclitaxel: 137–175 mg/m2 IV over 3 hours on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Forastiere AA, et al. Ann Oncol 1994;5 (Suppl 6):51–54.

2.16.3.3 Methotrexate

  • Methotrexate: 40 mg/m2 IV or IM weekly
  • Repeat cycle every week.

Hong WK, et al. N Engl J Med 1983;308:75–79.

2.16.3.4 Vinorelbine

  • Vinorelbine: 30 mg/m2 IV weekly
  • Repeat cycle every week.

Degardin M, et al. Ann Oncol 1998;9:1103–1107.

2.16.3.5 Cetuximab

  • Cetuximab: 400 mg/m2 IV loading dose, then 250 mg/m2 IV weekly
  • Repeat cycle every week.

Vermorken JB, et al. J Clin Oncol 2007;25:2171–2177.

2.16.3.6 Pembrolizumab

  • Pembrolizumab: 200 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 3 weeks.

Bauml J, et al. J Clin Oncol 2016;34:abstract 6011.

2.16.3.7 Nivolumab

  • Nivolumab: 240 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 14 days.

Ferris RL, et al. N Engl J Med 2016;375:1856–1867.

2.17 HEPATOCELLULAR CANCER

2.17.1 Combination Regimens

2.17.1.1 GEMOX

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Oxaliplatin: 100 mg/m2 IV on day 2
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks.

Taieb J, et al. Cancer 2003;98:2664–2670.

2.17.1.2 FOLFOX4

  • Oxaliplatin: 85 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • 5-Fluorouracil: 400 mg/m2 IV bolus, followed by 600 mg/m2 IV continuous infusion for 22 hours on days 1 and 2
  • Leucovorin: 200 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 2 as a 2-hour infusion before 5-fluorouracil
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks.

Qin S, et al. J Clin Oncol 2010:28; 303S (abstract 408).

2.17.1.3 Bevacizumab + Erlotinib

  • Bevacizumab: 10 mg/kg IV on days 1 and 14
  • Erlotinib: 150 mg PO daily
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Thomas MB, et al. J Clin Oncol 2009;27:843–850.

2.17.2 Single-Agent Regimens

2.17.2.1 Sorafenib

  • Sorafenib: 400 mg PO bid
  • Continue until disease progression. Dose may be reduced to 400 mg once daily or 400 mg every 2 days.

Llovet J, et al. N Engl J Med 2008;359:378–390.

2.17.2.2 Regorafenib

  • Regorafenib: 160 mg PO daily for 21 days
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Bruix J, et al. Lancet 2017;389:56–66.

2.17.2.3 Doxorubicin

  • Doxorubicin: 20–30 mg/m2 IV weekly
  • Repeat cycle every week.

Venook AP, et al. J Clin Oncol 1994;12:1323–1334.

2.17.2.4 Cisplatin

  • Cisplatin: 80 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every week.

Okada S, et al. Oncology 1993;50:22–26.

2.17.2.5 Capecitabine

  • Capecitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 PO bid on days 1–14
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days. Dose may be reduced to 825–900 mg/m2 PO bid on days 1–14. This dose reduction may decrease risk of toxicity without compromising clinical efficacy.

Patt YZ, et al. Cancer 2004;101:578–586.

2.17.2.6 Bevacizumab

  • Bevacizumab: 10 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 14 days.

Siegel AB, et al. J Clin Oncol 2008;26:2992–2998.

2.17.2.7 Pembrolizumab

  • Pembrolizumab: 10 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 14 days.

Zhu AX, et al. Lancet Oncol 2018. doi: 10.1016/S1470-2045(18)30351-6.

2.18 KAPOSI’S SARCOMA

2.18.1 Combination Regimens

2.18.1.1 BV

  • Bleomycin: 10 U/m2 IV on days 1 and 15
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 15 (maximum, 2 mg)
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks.

Ireland-Gill A, et al. Semin Oncol 1992;19 (Suppl 5):32–37.

2.18.1.2 ABV

  • Doxorubicin: 40 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Bleomycin: 15 U/m2 IV on days 1 and 15
  • Vinblastine: 6 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Laubenstein LL, et al. J Clin Oncol 1984;2:1115–1120.

2.18.2 Single-Agent Regimens

2.18.2.1 Daunorubicin liposome

  • Daunorubicin liposome: 40 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 14 days.

Gill PS, et al. J Clin Oncol 1996;14:2353–2364.

2.18.2.2 Doxorubicin liposome

  • Doxorubicin liposome: 20 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Northfelt DW, et al. J Clin Oncol 1997;15:653–659.

2.18.2.3 Paclitaxel

  • Paclitaxel: 135 mg/m2 IV over 3 hours on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Gill PS, et al. J Clin Oncol 1999;17:1876–1880.

or - Paclitaxel: 100 mg/m2 IV over 3 hours on day 1 - Repeat cycle every 2 weeks.

Gill PS, et al. Cancer 2002;95:147–154.

2.18.2.4 Docetaxel

  • Docetaxel: 25 mg/m2 IV weekly for 8 weeks, then every other week
  • Continue until disease progression.

Lim ST, et al. Cancer 2005;103:417–421.

2.18.2.5 Etoposide

  • Etoposide: 50 mg PO daily on days 1–7
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks.

Evans SR, et al. J Clin Oncol 2002;20:3236–3241.

2.18.2.6 Vinorelbine

  • Vinorelbine: 30 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks.

Nasti G, et al. J Clin Oncol 2000;18:1550–1557.

2.18.2.7 Interferon-alpha

  • Interferon alpha-2a: 36 million IU/m2 SC or IM, daily for 8–12 weeks.

Real FX, et al. J Clin Oncol 1986;4:544–551.

  • Interferon alpha-2b: 30 million IU/m2 SC or IM, 3 times weekly.

Groopman JE, et al. Ann Intern Med 1984;100:671–676.

2.19 LEUKEMIA

2.19.1 Acute Lymphocytic Leukemia - Induction Therapy

2.19.1.1 Linker Regimen

  • Daunorubicin: 50 mg/m2 IV every 24 hours on days 1–3
  • Vincristine: 2 mg IV on days 1, 8, 15, and 22
  • Prednisone: 60 mg/m2 PO divided into 3 doses on days 1–28
  • L-Asparaginase: 6,000 U/m2 IM on days 17–28
  • If bone marrow on day 14 is positive for residual leukemia,
  • Daunorubicin: 50 mg/m2 IV on day 15
  • If bone marrow on day 28 is positive for residual leukemia,
  • Daunorubicin: 50 mg/m2 IV on days 29 and 30
  • Vincristine: 2 mg IV on days 29 and 36
  • Prednisone: 60 mg/m2 PO on days 29–42
  • L-Asparaginase: 6,000 U/m2 IM on days 29–35

Linker CA, et al. Blood 1987;69:1242–1248. Linker CA, et al. Blood 1991;78:2814–2822.

2.19.2 Acute Lymphocytic Leukemia - Consolidation Therapy

2.19.2.1 Linker Regimen

  • Treatment A (cycles 1, 3, 5, and 7)
  • Daunorubicin: 50 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 2
  • Vincristine: 2 mg IV on days 1 and 8
  • Prednisone: 60 mg/m2 PO on days 1–14
  • L-Asparaginase: 12,000 U/m2 on days 2, 4, 7, 9, 11, and 14
  • Treatment B (cycles 2, 4, 6, and 8)
  • Teniposide: 165 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 4, 8, and 11
  • Cytarabine: 300 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 4, 8, and 11
  • Treatment C (cycle 9)
  • Methotrexate: 690 mg/m2 IV over 42 hours
  • Leucovorin: 15 mg/m2 IV every 6 hours for 12 doses beginning at 42 hours

Linker CA, et al. Blood 1987;69:1242–1248. Linker CA, et al. Blood 1991;78:2814–2822.

2.19.3 Acute Lymphocytic Leukemia - Maintenance Therapy

2.19.3.1 Linker Regimen

  • Methotrexate: 20 mg/m2 PO weekly
  • 6-Mercaptopurine: 75 mg/m2 PO daily
  • Continue for a total of 30 months of complete response.

Linker CA, et al. Blood 1987;69:1242–1248. Linker CA, et al. Blood 1991;78:2814–2822.

2.19.3.2 CNS Prophylaxis

  • Cranial irradiation: 1,800 cGy in 10 fractions over 12–14 days
  • Methotrexate: 12 mg IT weekly for 6 weeks
  • Begin within 1 week of complete response.
  • In patients with documented CNS involvement at time of diagnosis, intrathecal chemotherapy should begin during induction chemotherapy.
  • Methotrexate: 12 mg IT weekly for 10 doses
  • Cranial irradiation: 2,800 cGy

2.19.4 Acute Lymphocytic Leukemia - Induction Therapy

2.19.4.1 Larson Regimen

  • Induction (weeks 1–4)
    • Cyclophosphamide: 1,200 mg/m2 IV on day 1
    • Daunorubicin: 45 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
    • Vincristine: 2 mg IV on days 1, 8, 15, and 22
    • Prednisone: 60 mg/m2/day PO on days 1–21
    • L-Asparaginase: 6,000 U/m2 SC on days 5, 8, 11, 15, 18, 22
  • Early Intensification (weeks 5–12)
    • Methotrexate: 15 mg IT on day 1
    • Cyclophosphamide: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on day 1
    • 6-Mercaptopurine: 60 mg/m2/day PO on days 1–14
    • Cytarabine: 75 mg/m2 IV on days 1–4 and 8–11
    • Vincristine: 2 mg IV on days 15 and 22
    • L-Asparaginase: 6,000 U/m2 SC on days 15, 18, 22, and 25
    • Repeat the early intensification cycle once.
  • CNS Prophylaxis and Interim Maintenance (weeks 13–25)
    • Cranial irradiation: 2,400 cGy on days 1–12
    • Methotrexate: 15 mg IT on days 1, 8, 15, 22, and 29
    • 6-Mercaptopurine: 60 mg/m2/day PO on days 1–70
    • Methotrexate: 20 mg/m2 PO on days 36, 43, 50, 57, and 64
  • Late Intensification (weeks 26–33)
    • Doxorubicin: 30 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
    • Vincristine: 2 mg IV on days 1, 8, and 15
    • Dexamethasone: 10 mg/m2/day PO on days 1–14
    • Cyclophosphamide: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on day 29
    • 6-Thioguanine: 60 mg/m2/day PO on days 29–42
    • Cytarabine: 75 mg/m2 on days 29, 32, 36–39
  • Prolonged Maintenance (continue until 24 months after diagnosis)
    • Vincristine: 2 mg IV on day 1
    • Prednisone: 60 mg/m2/day PO on days 1–5
    • Methotrexate: 20 mg/m2 PO on days 1, 8, 15, and 22
    • 6-Mercaptopurine: 80 mg/m2/day PO on days 1–28
    • Repeat maintenance cycle every 28 days.

Larson R, et al. Blood 1995;85:2025–2037.

2.19.4.2 Hyper-CVAD Regimen

  • Cyclophosphamide: 300 mg/m2 IV every 12 hours for 6 doses on days 1–3
  • Mesna: 600 mg/m2 IV over 24 hours on days 1–3 ending 6 hours after the last dose of cyclophosphamide
  • Vincristine: 2 mg IV on days 4 and 11
  • Doxorubicin: 50 mg/m2 IV on day 4
  • Dexamethasone: 40 mg PO or IV on days 1–4 and 11–14
  • Alternate cycles every 21 days with the following:
  • Methotrexate: 200 mg/m2 IV over 2 hours, followed by 800 mg/m2 IV over 24 hours on day 1
  • Leucovorin: 15 mg IV every 6 hours for 8 doses, starting 24 hours after the completion of methotrexate infusion
  • Cytarabine: 3,000 mg/m2 IV every 12 hours for 4 doses on days 2–3
  • Methylprednisolone: 50 mg IV bid on days 1–3
  • Alternate 4 cycles of hyper-CVAD with 4 cycles of high-dose methotrexate and cytarabine therapy.

Kantarjian HM, et al. J Clin Oncol 2000;18:547–561.

2.19.4.3 CNS Prophylaxis

  • Methotrexate: 12 mg IT on day 2
  • Cytarabine: 100 mg IT on day 8
  • Repeat with each cycle of chemotherapy, depending on the risk of CNS disease.

2.19.4.4 Supportive Care

  • Ciprofloxacin: 500 mg PO bid
  • Fluconazole: 200 mg/day PO
  • Acyclovir: 200 mg PO bid
  • G-CSF: 10 µg/kg/day starting 24 hours after the end of chemotherapy (i.e., on day 5 of hyper-CVAD therapy and on day 4 of high-dose methotrexate and cytarabine therapy)

2.19.5 Acute Lymphocytic Leukemia - Single-Agent Regimens

2.19.5.1 Clofarabine

  • Clofarabine: 52 mg/m2 IV for 5 days
  • Repeat cycle every 2–6 weeks.

Faderl S, et al. Cancer 2005;103:1985–1995.

2.19.5.2 Nelarabine

  • Nelarabine: 1.5 g/m2/day IV on days 1, 3, and 5
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days up to a total of 4 cycles.

DeAngelo DJ, et al. Blood 2007;109:5136–5142.

2.19.5.3 Imatinib

  • Imatinib: 600 mg PO daily
  • Continue until disease progression.

Ottman OG, et al. Blood 2002;100:1965–1971.

2.19.5.4 Dasatinib

  • Dasatinib: 70 mg PO bid
  • Continue until disease progression.

Talpaz M, et al. N Engl J Med 2006;354:2531–2541.

2.19.5.5 Nilotinib

  • Nilotinib: 400–600 mg PO bid
  • Continue until disease progression.

Kantarjian HM, et al. N Engl J Med 2006;354:2542–2551.

2.19.5.6 Blinatumomab

  • Blinatumomab: 9 µg IV on days 1–7 and 28 µg IV on days 8–28 on cycle 1; 28 µg on days 1–28 on all subsequent cycles
  • Repeat cycle every 42 days.

Topp MS, et al. Lancet Oncol 2015;16:57–66.

2.19.5.7 Inotuzumab

  • Inotuzumab: 0.8 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.
  • For patients who achieve CR or CRi:
    • Inotuzumab: 0.5 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
    • Repeat cycle every 28 days.
  • For patients who do not achieve CR or CRi:
    • Inotuzumab: 0.8 mg/m2 IV on day 1 0.5 mg/m2 IV on days 8 and 15
    • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Kantarjian H, et al. N Engl J Med 2016;375:740–753.

2.19.6 Acute Myelogenous Leukemia - Induction Regimens

2.19.6.1 Ara-C + Daunorubicin (7 + 3)

  • Cytarabine: 100 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–7
  • Daunorubicin: 45 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3

Yates JW, et al. Cancer Chemother Rep 1973;57:485–488.

2.19.6.2 Liposomal Daunorubicin and Cytarabine

  • Liposomal daunorubicin and cytarabine: 100 U/m2 (44 mg/m2 daunorubicin and 100 mg/m2 cytarabine) IV on days 1, 3, and 5
  • A second induction course and up to 2 cycles of consolidation therapy can be given.

Lancet JE, et al. Blood 2014;123:3239–3246.

2.19.6.3 Ara-C + Daunorubicin + Gemtuzumab

  • Cytarabine: 200 mg/m2 IV on days 1–7
  • Daunorubicin: 60 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Gemtuzumab: 3 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 4, and 7

Goodwin CD, et al. Leukemia 2017;31:1855–1868.

2.19.6.4 Ara-C + Idarubicin

  • Cytarabine: 100 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–7
  • Idarubicin: 12 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3

Preisler H, et al. Blood 1987;69:1441–1449.

2.19.6.5 Ara-C + Doxorubicin

  • Cytarabine: 100 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–7
  • Doxorubicin: 30 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3

Preisler H, et al. Cancer Treat Rep 1977;61:89–92.

2.19.6.6 Ara-C + Clofarabine

  • Clofarabine: 40 mg/m2 IV over 1 hour on days 2–6
  • Cytarabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV over 2 hours on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycles every 4–6 weeks for up to a total of 3 cycles.

Faderi S, et al. Blood 2006;108:45–51.

2.19.6.7 Ara-C + Daunorubicin + Midostaurin

  • Cytarabine: 200 mg/m2 IV on days 1–7
  • Daunorubicin: 60 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Midostaurin: 50 mg/m2 PO bid on days 8–21
  • In patients who achieve a complete remission after induction therapy, they should then receive consolidation therapy

2.19.7 Acute Myelogenous Leukemia - Consolidation

  • Cytarabine: 3,000 mg/m2 IV every 12 hours on days 1, 3, and 5
  • Midostaurin: 50 mg/m2 PO bid on days 8–21
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for a total of 4 cycles of consolidation therapy.
  • In patients who remain in complete remission after completion of consolidation therapy, they then receive maintenance therapy

2.19.8 Acute Myelogenous Leukemia - Maintenance

  • Midostaurin: 50 mg/m2 PO bid
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for a total of 12 cycles.

Stone RM, et al. N Engl J Med 2017; doi: 10.1056/NEJMoa1614359.

2.19.8.1 AIDA (acute promyelocytic leukemia only)

  • ATRA: 45 mg/m2 PO daily
  • Idarubicin: 12 mg/m2 IV on days 2, 4, 6, and 8

Amadori S, et al. J Clin Oncol;34:972–979.

2.19.8.2 Tretinoin + Daunorubicin + Cytarabine (acute promyelocytic leukemia)

  • ATRA: 45 mg/m2 PO daily
  • Daunorubicin: 60 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Cytarabine: 200 mg/m2 IV on days 1–7

Sanz MA, et al. Blood 2010;115:5137–5146.

2.19.8.3 Tretinoin + Arsenic trioxide (acute promyelocytic leukemia)

  • ATRA: 45 mg/m2 PO daily
  • Arsenic trioxide: 0.15 mg/kg/day IV starting on day 10
  • Continue treatment until CR. Once in CR, patients receive the following:
  • ATRA: 45 mg/m2 PO daily on weeks 1–2, 5–6, 9–10, 13–14, 17–18, 21–22, and 25–26
  • Arsenic trioxide: 0.15 mg/kg/day IV on Monday–Friday on weeks 1–4, 9–12, 17–20, and 25–28
  • Therapy should be terminated 28 weeks after the CR date.

Estey E, et al. Blood 2006;107:3469–3473.

2.19.8.4 Mitoxantrone + Etoposide (salvage regimen)

  • Mitoxantrone: 10 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–5
  • Etoposide: 100 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–5

Ho AD, et al. J Clin Oncol 1988;6:213–217.

2.19.8.5 FLAG

  • Fludarabine: 30 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Cytarabine: 2,000 mg/m2/day IV over 4 hours on days 1–5 starting 3.5 hours after fludarabine
  • G-CSF: 5 µg/kg/day SC starting 24 hours before chemotherapy
  • An additional cycle may be given in the setting of a partial response.

Montillo M, et al. Am J Hematol 1998;58:105–109.

2.19.9 Acute Myelogenous Leukemia - Consolidation Regimens

2.19.9.1 Ara-C + Daunorubicin (5 + 2)

  • Cytarabine: 100 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–5
  • Daunorubicin: 45 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 2

Wiernik PH, et al. Blood 1992;79:313–319.

2.19.9.2 Liposomal Daunorubicin and Cytarabine

  • Liposomal daunorubicin and cytarabine: 29 mg/m2 daunorubicin and 65 mg/m2 cytarabine on days 1 and 3

Lancet JE, et al. Blood 2014;123:3239–3246.

2.19.9.3 Ara-C + Idarubicin

  • Cytarabine: 100 mg/m2 IV continuous infusion on days 1–5
  • Idarubicin: 13 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 2
  • Repeat cycle every 21–28 days.

Tallman MS, et al. Blood 2005;106:1154–1163.

2.19.10 Acute Myelogenous Leukemia - Single-Agent Regimens

2.19.10.1 Cladribine

  • Cladribine: 0.1 mg/kg/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–7

Santana VM, et al. J Clin Oncol 1992;10:364–369.

2.19.10.2 High-Dose Cytarabine

  • Cytarabine: 1,500–3,000 mg/m2 IV over 3 hours, every 12 hours on days 1, 3, and 5
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Gardin C, et al. Blood 2007;109:5129–5132.

2.19.10.3 Clofarabine

  • Clofarabine: 40 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 3–6 weeks.

Kantarjian HM, et al. Blood 2003;102:2379–2386.

2.19.10.4 Tretinoin (acute promyelocytic leukemia only)

Tretinoin: 45 mg/m2 PO daily in 1–2 divided doses

Degos L, et al. Blood 1995;85:2643–2653.

2.19.10.5 Arsenic trioxide (acute promyelocytic leukemia only)

  • Arsenic trioxide: 0.15 mg/kg IV daily

Soignet SL, et al. J Clin Oncol 2001;19:3852–3860.

  • Continue until bone marrow remission up to a maximum of 60 doses. Patients who meet the criteria for clinical CR can receive an additional course of arsenic trioxide as consolidation beginning 3–4 weeks after completion of induction therapy up to a cumulative total of 25 doses.

Sievers EL, et al. Blood 1999;11:3678–3684.

2.19.10.6 Sorafenib

  • Sorafenib: 200-400 mg PO bid
  • Continue until disease progression or stem cell transplant.

Man CH, et al. Blood 2012;119:5133–5143.

2.19.10.7 Azacitidine

  • Azacitidine: 75 mg/m2 SC daily for 7 days
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for at least 6 cycles.

Fenaux P, et al. J Clin Oncol 2010;28:562–569.

2.19.10.8 Decitabine

  • Decitabine: 20 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 4 weeks.

Kantarjian HM, et al. J Clin Oncol 2012;30:2670–2677.

2.19.10.9 Enasidenib

  • Enasidenib: 100 mg PO daily
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Stein EM, et al. Blood 2017;130:722–731.

2.19.11 Chronic Lymphocytic Leukemia - Combination Regimens

2.19.11.1 CVP

  • Cyclophosphamide: 400 mg/m2 PO on days 1–5 (or 800 mg/m2 IV on day 1)
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on day 1 (maximum dose, 2 mg)
  • Prednisone: 100 mg/m2 PO on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Raphael B, et al. J Clin Oncol 1991;9:770–776.

2.19.11.2 CF

  • Cyclophosphamide: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Fludarabine: 20 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Trimethoprim/sulfamethoxazole (Bactrim DS) 1 tablet PO bid
  • Repeat cycle every 21–28 days.

Keating MJ, et al. Blood 1998;92:1165–1171.

2.19.11.3 FP

  • Fludarabine: 30 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Prednisone: 30 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

O’Brien S, et al. Blood 1993;82:1695–1700.

2.19.11.4 CP

  • Chlorambucil: 30 mg/m2 PO on day 1
  • Prednisone: 80 mg PO on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Raphael B, et al. J Clin Oncol 1991;9:770–776.

2.19.11.5 FR

  • Fludarabine: 25 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 4 of cycle 1 and then on day 1 thereafter
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for 6 cycles.

Byrd JC, et al. Blood 2003;101:6–14. Byrd JC, et al. J Clin Oncol 2011;29:1349–1355.

2.19.11.6 FCR

  • Fludarabine: 25 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Cyclophosphamide: 250 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for 6 cycles. On cycles 2–6, rituximab is given at 500 mg/m2.

Keating M, et al. J Clin Oncol 2005;22:4079–4088.

2.19.11.7 PCR

  • Pentostatin: 2 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cyclophosphamide: 600 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Kay NE, et al. Blood 2004;104 (abstract 339).

2.19.11.8 Bendamustine + Rituximab

  • Bendamustine: 90 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 2
  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 0 of cycle 1, then 500 mg/m2 IV on day 1 of cycles 2–6
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for up to 6 cycles.

Byrd JC, et al. J Clin Oncol 2014;32:3039–3047.

2.19.11.9 Venetoclax + Rituximab

  • Venetoclax: 20 mg/day PO on days 1–7, 50 mg/day PO on days 8–14, 100 mg/day PO on days 15–21, 200 mg/day PO on days 22–28, and then 400 mg/day PO daily
  • Venetoclax: 400 mg PO daily
  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 1 of cycle 1, then 500 mg/m2 IV on day 1 of cycles 2–6
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for up to 6 cycles. After cycle 6, venetoclax is continued at 400 mg PO daily for up to 2 years.

Seymour JF, et al. N Engl J Med 2018;378:1107–1120.

2.19.11.10 Idelasib + Rituximab

  • Idelasib: 150 mg PO bid
  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 1, then 500 mg/m2 IV every 2 weeks for 4 doses and then every 4 weeks for 3 doses for a total of 8 doses

Furman RR, et al. N Engl J Med 2014;370:997–1007.

2.19.11.11 Obinutuzumab + Chlorambucil

  • Obinutuzumab: 100 mg IV on day 1, cycle 1; 900 mg IV on day 2, cycle 1; 1,000 mg IV on days 8 and 15 of cycle 1; 1,000 mg IV on day 1 of cycles 2–6
  • Chlorambucil: 0.5 mg/kg PO on days 1 and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Goede V, et al. N Engl J Med 2014;370:1101–1110.

2.19.12 Chronic Lymphocytic Leukemia - Single-Agent Regimens

2.19.12.1 Alemtuzumab

  • Alemtuzumab: 30 mg/day IV, 3 times per week
  • Repeat weekly for up to a maximum of 23 weeks. Premedicate with diphenhydramine 50 mg PO and acetaminophen 625 mg PO 30 minutes before drug infusion. Patients should be placed on trimethoprim/sulfamethoxazole (Bactrim DS) PO bid and famciclovir 250 mg PO bid from day 8 through 2 months following completion of therapy.

Osterborg A, et al. J Clin Oncol 1997;15:1567–1574.

2.19.12.2 Chlorambucil

  • Chlorambucil: 6–14 mg/day PO as induction therapy and then 0.7 mg/kg PO for 2–4 days
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Dighiero G, et al. N Engl J Med 1998;338:1506–1514.

2.19.12.3 Cladribine

  • Cladribine: 0.09 mg/kg/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–7
  • Repeat cycle every 28–35 days.

Saven A, et al. J Clin Oncol 1995;13:570–574.

2.19.12.4 Fludarabine

  • Fludarabine: 20–30 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Keating MJ, et al. Blood 1988;92:1165–1171.

2.19.12.5 Prednisone

  • Prednisone: 20–30 mg/m2/day PO for 1–3 weeks.

Sawitsky A, et al. Blood 1977;50:1049.

2.19.12.6 Rituximab

  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV weekly for 4 weeks
  • Repeat cycle every 6 months for a total of 4 courses.

Hainsworth JD, et al. J Clin Oncol 2003;21:1746–1751.

2.19.12.7 Ofatumumab

  • Ofatumumab: 300 mg IV initial dose followed 1 week later by 2,000 mg IV weekly dose for 7 doses, followed 4 weeks later by 2,000 mg IV every 4 weeks for 4 doses.
  • A total of 12 doses is recommended.

Wierda WG, et al. J Clin Oncol 2010;28:1749–1755.

2.19.12.8 Pentostatin

  • Pentostatin: 4 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 14 days.

Grever MR, et al. J Clin Oncol 1985;3:1196–1201.

2.19.12.9 Bendamustine

  • Bendamustine: 100 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 2
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for up to 6 cycles.

Alvado M, et al. Semin Oncol 2002;29(4 Suppl 13):19–22.

or - Bendamustine: 60 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5 - Repeat cycle every 28 days. In patients >70 years, use dose of 50 mg/m2.

Kath R, et al. J Cancer Res Clin Oncol 2001;127:48–54.

2.19.12.10 Lenalidomide

  • Lenalidomide: 10 mg PO daily on days 1–28
  • Increase dose by 5 mg every 28 days up to a maximum of 25 mg daily until disease progression or toxicity.

Ferrajoli A, et al. Blood 2008;111:5291–5297.

2.19.12.11 Ibrutinib

  • Ibrutinib: 560 mg PO daily
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Byrd JC, et al. N Engl J Med 2014;369:32–42.

2.19.12.12 Venetoclax

  • Venetoclax: 20 mg/day PO on days 1–7, 50 mg/day PO on days 8–14, 100 mg/day PO on days 15–21, 200 mg/day PO on days 22–28, and then 400 mg/day PO daily
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Stilgenbauer S, et al. Lancet Oncol 2016;17:768–778.

2.19.13 Chronic Myelogenous Leukemia - Combination Regimens

2.19.13.1 Interferon + Cytarabine

  • Interferon a-2b: 5 million U/m2 SC daily
  • Cytarabine: 20 mg/m2 SC daily for 10 days
  • Repeat cytarabine on a monthly basis. The dose of interferon should be reduced by 50% when the neutrophil count drops below 1,500/mm3, the platelet count drops below 100,000/m3, or both. Interferon and cytarabine should both be discontinued when the neutrophil count drops below 1,000/mm3, platelet count drops below 50,000/mm3, or both.

Guilhot F, et al. N Engl J Med 1997;337:223–229.

2.19.14 Chronic Myelogenous Leukemia - Single-Agent Regimens

2.19.14.1 Imatinib

  • Imatinib: 400 mg/day PO (chronic phase); 600 mg/day PO (accelerated phase blast crisis)

Druker BJ, et al. N Engl J Med 2001;344:1031–1037.

2.19.14.2 Dasatinib

  • Dasatinib: 70 mg PO bid

Kantarjian HM, et al. Blood 2007;110:3540–3546.

or - Dasatinib: 100 mg PO daily

Kantarjian HM, et al. N Engl J Med 2010;362:2260–2270.

2.19.14.3 Nilotinib

  • Nilotinib: 400 mg PO bid

Kantarjian HM, et al. Blood 2007;109:5143–5150.

or - Nilotinib: 300 mg PO bid

Saglio G, et al. N Engl J Med 2010;362:2251–2259.

2.19.14.4 Bosutinib

  • Bosutinib: 500 mg PO daily

Khoury HJ, et al. Blood 2012;119:3403–3412.

2.19.14.5 Ponatinib

  • Ponatinib: 45 mg PO bid

Kantarjian HM, et al. Blood 2012;120 (abstract 915).

2.19.14.6 Busulfan

  • Busulfan: 1.8 mg/m2/day PO

Hehlmann R, et al. Blood 1993;82:398–407.

2.19.14.7 Hydroxyurea

  • Hydroxyurea: 1–5 g/day PO

Hehlmann R, et al. Blood 1994;84:4064–4077.

2.19.14.8 Interferon alpha-2a

  • Interferon alpha-2a: 9 million U/day SC

The Italian Cooperative Study Group on Chronic Myelogenous Leukemia. N Engl J Med 1994;330:820–825.

2.19.14.9 Omacetaxine

  • Omacetaxine: 1.25 mg/m2 SC bid on days 1–14 for first cycle and induction phase followed by 1.25 mg/m2 SC bid on days 1–7 as maintenance phase
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Cortes J, et al. Blood 2012;120:2573–2581.

2.19.15 Hairy Cell Leukemia - Single-Agent Regimens

2.19.15.1 Cladribine

  • Cladribine: 0.09 mg/kg/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–7
  • Administer one cycle.

Saven A, et al. Blood 1992;79:111–1120.

2.19.15.2 Pentostatin

  • Pentostatin: 4 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 14 days for 6 cycles.

Cassileth PA, et al. J Clin Oncol 1991;9:243–246.

2.19.15.3 Interferon alpha-2a

  • Interferon alpha-2a: 3 million U SC or IM, 3 times per week
  • Continue treatment for up to 1 to 1.5 years.

Ratain MJ, et al. Blood 1985;65:644–648.

2.20 LUNG CANCER

2.20.1 Non–Small Cell Lung Cancer - Combined Modality Therapy

2.20.1.1 Cisplatin + Etoposide + Radiation Therapy

  • Cisplatin: 50 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, 29, and 36
  • Etoposide: 50 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5 and 29–33
  • Radiation therapy: 180 cGy/day for a total dose of 4500 cGy
  • Chemotherapy is given concurrently with radiation therapy.

Gandara DR, et al. J Clin Oncol 2003;21:2004–2010.

2.20.1.2 Weekly Carboplatin + Paclitaxel + Radiation Therapy

  • Paclitaxel: 45 mg/m2 IV weekly for 7 weeks
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 2, IV weekly for 7 weeks
  • Radiation therapy: 200 cGy/day for a total dose of 6300 cGy over 7 weeks
  • Chemotherapy is given concurrently with radiation therapy. Three to 4 weeks after the completion of chemoradiotherapy, two additional cycles of the following chemotherapy are given:
  • Paclitaxel: 200 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for 2 cycles.

Belani CP, et al. J Clin Oncol 2005;23:5883–5891.

2.20.2 Non–Small Cell Lung Cancer - Adjuvant Therapy - Combination Regimens

2.20.2.1 Paclitaxel + Carboplatin

  • Paclitaxel: 175 mg/m2 IV over 3 hours on day 1
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for 4 cycles.

Strauss GM, et al. J Clin Oncol 2004; 621S (abstract 7019).

2.20.2.2 Vinorelbine + Cisplatin

  • Vinorelbine: 25 mg/m2 IV weekly for 16 weeks
  • Cisplatin: 50 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for 4 cycles.

Winton T, et al. N Engl J Med 2005;352:2589–2597.

2.20.2.3 Cisplatin + Vinblastine

  • Cisplatin: 100 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vinblastine: 4 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, 15, 22, and 29, then every 2 weeks after day 43
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for 4 cycles.

Arriagada R, et al. N Engl J Med 2004:350:351–360.

2.20.2.4 Etoposide + Cisplatin

  • Etoposide: 100 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Cisplatin: 100 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for 4 cycles.

Arriagada R, et al. N Engl J Med 2004:350:351–360.

2.20.2.5 Pemetrexed + Cisplatin

  • Pemetrexed: 500 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cisplatin: 80 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for 6 cycles. Folic acid at 350–1,000 µg PO q day beginning 1 week prior to therapy and vitamin B12 at 1,000 µg IM beginning 1–2 weeks prior to first dose of therapy and repeated every 9 weeks. Dexamethasone at 4 mg PO bid on the day before, the day of, and the day after pemetrexed.

Kreuter M, et al. Ann Oncol 2012;24:986–992.

2.20.3 Non–Small Cell Lung Cancer - Metastatic Disease - Combination Regimens

2.20.3.1 Carboplatin + Paclitaxel (PC)

  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Paclitaxel: 200 mg/m2 IV over 3 hours on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Sandler AB, et al. N Engl J Med 2006;355:2542–2560.

2.20.3.2 Carboplatin + Nab-Paclitaxel

  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Nab-Paclitaxel: 100 mg/m2 IV weekly on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Socinski ME, et al. J Clin Oncol 2012; 30:2055–2062.

2.20.3.3 Carboplatin + Paclitaxel (weekly regimen)

  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Paclitaxel: 100 mg/m2 IV weekly for 3 weeks
  • Repeat cycle every 4 weeks up to 4 cycles. If response or stable disease, may then treat with maintenance chemotherapy of:
  • Paclitaxel: 70 mg/m2 IV weekly for 3 weeks
  • Continue until disease progression.

Belani CP, et al. J Clin Oncol 2008;26:468–473.

2.20.3.4 Carboplatin + Paclitaxel + Bevacizumab (PCB)

  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Paclitaxel: 200 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Bevacizumab: 15 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Sandler AB, et al. N Engl J Med 2006;355:2542–2560.

2.20.3.5 Gemcitabine + Cisplatin + Bevacizumab (GCB)

  • Gemcitabine: 1,250 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Cisplatin: 80 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Bevacizumab: 7.5 or 15 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for a total of 6 cycles.

Reck M, et al. J Clin Oncol 2009;27:1227–1234.

2.20.3.6 Cisplatin + Paclitaxel

  • Cisplatin: 80 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Paclitaxel: 175 mg/m2 IV over 3 hours on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Giaccone G, et al. J Clin Oncol 1998;16:2133–2141.

2.20.3.7 Docetaxel + Carboplatin

  • Docetaxel: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Fossella F, et al. J Clin Oncol 2003;21:3016–3024.

2.20.3.8 Docetaxel + Cisplatin

  • Docetaxel: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cisplatin: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Belani CP, et al. Clin Lung Cancer 1999;1:144–150.

2.20.3.9 Docetaxel + Gemcitabine

  • Docetaxel: 100 mg/m2 IV on day 8
  • Gemcitabine: 1,100 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days. G-CSF support is required from day 9 to day 15.

Georgoulias V, et al. Lancet 2001;357:1478–1484.

2.20.3.10 Gemcitabine + Cisplatin

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Cisplatin: 100 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Abratt RP, et al. J Clin Oncol 1997;15:744–749.

2.20.3.11 Gemcitabine + Carboplatin

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 5, IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Langer CJ, et al. Semin Oncol 1999;26 (Suppl 4):12–18.

2.20.3.12 Gemcitabine + Vinorelbine

  • Gemcitabine: 1,200 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Vinorelbine: 30 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Frasci G, et al. J Clin Oncol 2000;18:2529–2536.

2.20.3.13 Vinorelbine + Cisplatin

  • Vinorelbine: 30 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Cisplatin: 120 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Smith TJ, et al. J Clin Oncol 1995;13:2166–2173.

2.20.3.14 Vinorelbine + Cisplatin + Cetuximab

  • Vinorelbine: 25 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Cisplatin: 80 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cetuximab: 400 mg/m2 IV loading dose, then 250 mg/m2 IV weekly
  • Repeat cycle every 3 weeks up to 6 cycles.

Pirker R, et al. Proc Am Soc Clin Oncol 2008;26 (abstract 3).

2.20.3.15 Vinorelbine + Carboplatin

  • Vinorelbine: 25 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Cremonesi M, et al. Oncology 2003;64:97–101.

2.20.3.16 Pemetrexed + Cisplatin

  • Pemetrexed: 500 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cisplatin: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days up to 6 cycles. Folic acid at 350–1,000 µg PO q day beginning 1 week prior to therapy and vitamin B12 at 1,000 µg IM beginning 1–2 weeks prior to first dose of therapy and repeated every 9 weeks. Dexamethasone at 4 mg PO bid on the day before, the day of, and the day after pemetrexed.

Scagliotti GV, et al. J Clin Oncol 2008;21:3543–3551.

2.20.3.17 Pemetrexed + Carboplatin

  • Pemetrexed: 500 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 5, IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days up to 4 cycles. Folic acid at 350–1,000 µg PO q day beginning 1 week prior to therapy and vitamin B12 at 1,000 µg IM beginning 1–2 weeks prior to first dose of therapy and repeated every 9 weeks. Dexamethasone at 4 mg PO bid on the day before, the day of, and the day after pemetrexed.

Scagliotti GV. Semin Oncol 2005;32 (2 Suppl 2):S5–S8.

2.20.3.18 EP

  • Etoposide: 120 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Cisplatin: 60 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21–28 days.

Longeval E, et al. Cancer 1982;50:2751–2756.

2.20.3.19 EP + Docetaxel

  • Cisplatin: 50 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, 29, and 36
  • Etoposide: 50 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5 and 29–33
  • Administer concurrent thoracic radiotherapy, followed 4–6 weeks after the completion of combined modality therapy by
  • Docetaxel: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for 3 cycles. Dose of docetaxel can be escalated to 100 mg/m2 IV on subsequent cycles in the absence of toxicity.

Gandara D, et al. J Clin Oncol 2003;21:2004–2010.

2.20.3.20 Docetaxel + Bevacizumab

  • Docetaxel: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Bevacizumab: 15 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Herbst RS, et al. J Clin Oncol 2007;25:4734–4750.

2.20.3.21 Pemetrexed + Carboplatin + Bevacizumab

  • Pemetrexed: 500 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Bevacizumab: 15 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days up to 6 cycles. Folic acid at 350–1,000 µg PO q day beginning 1 week prior to therapy and vitamin B12 at 1,000 µg IM beginning 1–2 weeks prior to first dose of therapy and repeated every 9 weeks. Dexamethasone at 4 mg PO bid on the day before, the day of, and the day after pemetrexed.

Patel JD, et al. J Clin Oncol 2009;27:3284–3289.

2.20.3.22 Pemetrexed + Carboplatin + Pembrolizumab

  • Pemetrexed: 500 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 5, IV on day 1
  • Pembrolizumab: 200 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days up to 4 cycles. Followed by pembrolizumab maintenance therapy up to a total of 35 cycles and pemetrexed maintenance.
  • Folic acid at 350–1,000 µg PO q day beginning 1 week prior to therapy and vitamin B12 at 1,000 µg IM beginning 1–2 weeks prior to first dose of therapy and repeated every 9 weeks. Dexamethasone at 4 mg PO bid on the day before, the day of, and the day after pemetrexed.

Gandhi L, et al. N Engl J Med 2018;378:2078–2092.

2.20.3.23 Pemetrexed + Cisplatin + Pembrolizumab

  • Pemetrexed: 500 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cisplatin: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Pembrolizumab: 200 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days up to 4 cycles. Followed by pembrolizumab maintenance therapy up to a total of 35 cycles and pemetrexed maintenance.
  • Folic acid at 350–1,000 µg PO q day beginning 1 week prior to therapy and vitamin B12 at 1,000 µg IM beginning 1–2 weeks prior to first dose of therapy and repeated every 9 weeks. Dexamethasone at 4 mg PO bid on the day before, the day of, and the day after pemetrexed.

Gandhi L, et al. N Engl J Med 2018;378:2078–2092.

2.20.3.24 Cisplatin + Vinorelbine + Cetuximab

  • Cisplatin: 80 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vinorelbine: 25 mg/m2 IV continuous on days 1 and 8
  • Cetuximab: 400 mg/m2 IV loading dose, then 250 mg/m2 IV weekly
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days up to 6 cycles.

Pirker R, et al. Lancet 2009;373:1525–1531.

2.20.3.25 Platinum-Based Chemotherapy + Maintenance Pemetrexed (non-squamous histology)

  • Platinum-based chemotherapy × 4 cycles, followed by:
  • Pemetrexed: 500 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days up to 6 cycles. Folic acid at 350–1,000 µg PO q day beginning 1 week prior to therapy and vitamin B12 at 1,000 µg IM beginning 1–2 weeks prior to first dose of therapy and repeated every 9 weeks. Dexamethasone at 4 mg PO bid on the day before, the day of, and the day after pemetrexed.

Belani CP, et al. J Clin Oncol 2009;27:18S (abstract CRA8000).

2.20.3.26 Nab-Paclitaxel + Carboplatin

  • Nab-Paclitaxel: 100 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Socinski MA, et al. J Clin Oncol 2012;30:2055–2062.

2.20.3.27 Docetaxel + Ramucirumab

  • Docetaxel: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Ramucirumab: 10 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Garon EB, et al. Lancet 2014;384:665–673.

2.20.3.28 Gemcitabine + Cisplatin + Necitumumab

  • Gemcitabine: 1,250 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Cisplatin: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Necitumumab: 800 mg IV on days 1 and 8
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Thatcher N, et al. Lancet Oncol 2015;16:763–774.

2.20.3.29 Dabrafenib + Trametinib

  • Dabrafenib: 150 mg PO bid
  • Trametinib: 2 mg PO daily
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Planchard D, et al. Lancet Oncol 2016;17:642–650.

2.20.3.30 Carboplatin + Paclitaxel + Pembrolizumab

  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Paclitaxel: 200 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Pembrolizumab: 200 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for 4 cycles followed by pembrolizumab for up to a total of 35 treatments.

Paz-Ares LG, et al. J Clin Oncol 2018;36 (Suppl; abstr 105).

2.20.3.31 Carboplatin + Nab-Paclitaxel + Pembrolizumab

  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Nab-Paclitaxel: 100 mg/m2 IV weekly on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Pembrolizumab: 200 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for 4 cycles followed by pembrolizumab for up to a total of 35 treatments.

Paz-Ares LG, et al. J Clin Oncol 2018;36 (Suppl; abstr 105).

2.20.4 Non–Small Cell Lung Cancer - Metastatic Disease - Single-Agent Regimens

2.20.4.1 Paclitaxel

  • Paclitaxel: 225 mg/m2 IV over 3 hours on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Lilenbaum RC, et al. J Clin Oncol 2005;23:190–196.

or - Paclitaxel: 80–100 mg/m2 IV weekly for 3 weeks - Repeat cycle every 28 days after 1-week rest.

Tester WJ, et al. Cancer 1997;79:724–729.

2.20.4.2 Nab-Paclitaxel

  • Nab-Paclitaxel: 125 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Rizvi NA, et al. J Clin Oncol 2008;26:639–643.

2.20.4.3 Docetaxel

  • Docetaxel: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Miller VA, et al. Semin Oncol 2000;27 (Suppl 3):3–10.

or - Docetaxel: 36 mg/m2 IV weekly for 6 weeks - Repeat cycle every 8 weeks after 2-week rest. Premedicate with dexamethasone 8 mg PO at 12 hours and immediately before docetaxel infusion and 12 hours after each dose.

Hainsworth JD, et al. Cancer 2000;89:328–333.

2.20.4.4 Pemetrexed

  • Pemetrexed: 500 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days. Folic acid at 350–1,000 µg PO q day beginning 1 week prior to therapy and vitamin B12 at 1,000 µg IM beginning 1–2 weeks prior to first dose of therapy and repeated every 3 cycles.

Hanna N, et al. J Clin Oncol 2004;22:1589–1597.

2.20.4.5 Gemcitabine

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Manegold C, et al. Ann Oncol 1997;8:525–529.

2.20.4.6 Vinorelbine

  • Vinorelbine: 25 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 7 days.

Furuse K, et al. Ann Oncol 1996;7:815–820.

2.20.4.7 Gefitinib

  • Gefitinib: 250 mg/day PO
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Herbst RS. Semin Oncol 2003;30 (Suppl 1):30–38.

2.20.4.8 Erlotinib

  • Erlotinib: 150 mg/day PO
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Shepherd FA, et al. J Clin Oncol 2004;22 (Suppl 1):14S (abstract 7022).

2.20.4.9 Afatinib

  • Afatinib: 40 mg/day PO
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Sequist LV, et al. J Clin Oncol 2013;27:3327–3334.

2.20.4.10 Sunitinib

  • Sunitinib: 50 mg/day PO for 4 weeks
  • Repeat cycle every 6 weeks.

Socinski MA, et al. J Clin Oncol 2008;26:650–656.

2.20.4.11 Cetuximab

  • Cetuximab: 400 mg/m2 IV loading dose, then 250 mg/m2 IV weekly
  • Repeat cycle every week.

Hanna N, et al. J Clin Oncol 2006;24:5253–5258.

2.20.4.12 Nivolumab

  • Nivolumab: 240 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks. May also administer 480 mg IV on day 1 with cycles every 4 weeks.

Brahmer J, et al. N Engl J Med 2015;373:123–135.

2.20.4.13 Crizotinib

  • Crizotinib: 250 mg PO bid
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Kwak EL, et al. N Engl J Med 2010;363:1693–1703.

2.20.4.14 Ceritinib

  • Ceritinib: 750 mg/day PO
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Shaw AT, et al. N Engl J Med 2014;370:1189–1197.

2.20.4.15 Alectinib

  • Alectinib: 600 mg PO bid
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Shaw AT, et al. Lancet Oncol 2016;17:234–242.

2.20.4.16 Brigatinib

  • Brigatinib: 90 mg PO daily for 7 days and then 180 mg PO daily
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Kim DW, et al. J Clin Oncol 2017. doi: 10. 1200/JCO.2016.71.5904.

2.20.4.17 Osimertinib

  • Osimertinib: 80 mg/day PO
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Yang J, et al. J Thorac Oncl 2016;11:S152–153.

2.20.4.18 Pembrolizumab

  • Pembrolizumab: 200 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 3 weeks.

Mok T, et al. J Thorac Oncol 2016;11:S142.

2.20.4.19 Durvalumab

  • Durvalumab: 10 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 14 days.

Antonia SJ, et al. N Engl J Med 2017;377:1919–1929.

2.20.5 Small Cell Lung Cancer - Combination Regimens

2.20.5.1 EP

  • Etoposide: 80 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Cisplatin: 80 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Ihde DC, et al. J Clin Oncol 1994;12:2022–2034.

2.20.5.2 EC

  • Etoposide: 100 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Viren M, et al. Acta Oncol 1994;33:921–924.

2.20.5.3 Irinotecan + Cisplatin

  • Irinotecan: 60 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Cisplatin: 60 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Noda K, et al. N Engl J Med 2002;346:85–91.

2.20.5.4 Topotecan + Cisplatin

  • Topotecan: 1.7 mg/m2/day PO on days 1–5
  • Cisplatin: 60 mg/m2 IV on day 5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days up to 4 cycles or 2 cycles beyond best response.

Eckardt JR, et al. J Clin Oncol 2006;24:2044–2051.

2.20.5.5 Carboplatin + Paclitaxel + Etoposide

  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Paclitaxel: 200 mg/m2 IV over 1 hour on day 1
  • Etoposide: 50 mg alternating with 100 mg PO on days 1–10
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Hainsworth JD, et al. J Clin Oncol 1997;15:3464–3470.

2.20.5.6 Carboplatin + Paclitaxel

  • Carboplatin: AUC of 2, IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Paclitaxel: 80 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for 6 cycles.

Neubauer M, et al. J Clin Oncol 2004;22:1872–1877.

2.20.5.7 CAV

  • Cyclophosphamide: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Doxorubicin: 40 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 1 mg/m2 IV on day 1 (maximum, 2 mg)
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Roth BJ, et al. J Clin Oncol 1992;10:282–291.

2.20.5.8 CAE

  • Cyclophosphamide: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Doxorubicin: 45 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Etoposide: 50 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Aisner J, et al. Semin Oncol 1986;(Suppl 3):54–62.

2.20.6 Small Cell Lung Cancer - Single-Agent Regimens

2.20.6.1 Etoposide

  • Etoposide: 160 mg/m2 PO on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Johnson DH. Semin Oncol 1993;20:315–325.

or - Etoposide: 50 mg/m2/day PO on days 1–21 - Repeat cycle as tolerated.

Johnson DH, et al. J Clin Oncol 1990;8:1013–1017.

2.20.6.2 Paclitaxel

  • Paclitaxel: 80–100 mg/m2 IV weekly for 3 weeks
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Hainsworth JD, et al. Semin Oncol 1999;26 (Suppl 2):60–66.

2.20.6.3 Topotecan

  • Topotecan: 1.5 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Ardizzoni A, et al. J Clin Oncol 1997;15:2090–2096.

2.20.6.4 Gemcitabine

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 PO on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Masters GA, et al. J Clin Oncol 2003;21:1550–1555.

2.21 LYMPHOMA

2.21.1 Hodgkin’s Lymphoma - Combination Regimens

2.21.1.1 ABVD

  • Doxorubicin: 25 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 15
  • Bleomycin: 10 U/m2 IV on days 1 and 15
  • Vinblastine: 6 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 15
  • Dacarbazine: 375 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Bonadonna G, et al. Cancer 1975;36:252–259.

2.21.1.2 A + AVD

  • Brentuximab: 1.2 mg/kg IV on days 1 and 15
  • Doxorubicin: 25 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 15
  • Vinblastine: 6 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 15
  • Dacarbazine: 375 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Connors JM, et al. N Engl J Med 2018;378:331–344.

2.21.1.3 MOPP

  • Nitrogen mustard: 6 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Procarbazine: 100 mg/m2 PO on days 1–14
  • Prednisone: 40 mg/m2 PO on days 1–14
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

DeVita VT Jr, et al. Ann Intern Med 1970;73:881–895.

2.21.1.4 MOPP/ABVD Hybrid

  • Nitrogen mustard: 6 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on day 1 (maximum dose, 2 mg)
  • Procarbazine: 100 mg/m2 PO on days 1–14
  • Prednisone: 40 mg/m2 PO on days 1–14
  • Doxorubicin: 35 mg/m2 IV on day 8
  • Bleomycin: 10 U/m2 IV on day 8
  • Hydrocortisone: 100 mg IV given before bleomycin
  • Vinblastine: 6 mg/m2 IV on day 8
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Klimo P, et al. J Clin Oncol 1985;3:1174–1182.

2.21.1.5 MOPP Alternating with ABVD

  • See MOPP and ABVD regimens outlined above.

2.21.1.6 Stanford V

  • Nitrogen mustard: 6 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Doxorubicin: 25 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 15
  • Vinblastine: 6 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 15
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on days 8 and 22
  • Bleomycin: 5 U/m2 IV on days 8 and 22
  • Etoposide: 60 mg/m2 IV on days 15 and 16
  • Prednisone: 40 mg PO every other day
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days. In patients >50 years of age, vinblastine dose reduced to 4 mg/m2 and vincristine dose reduced to 1 mg/m2 on weeks 9 and 12.
  • Dose of prednisone tapered starting on week 10. Patient should be placed on prophylactic trimethoprim/sulfamethoxazole (Bactrim DS) PO bid and acyclovir 200 mg PO tid.

Bartlett NL, et al. J Clin Oncol 1995;13:1080–1088.

2.21.1.7 EVA

  • Etoposide: 100 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Vinblastine: 6 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Doxorubicin: 50 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for up to 6 cycles.

Canellos GP, et al. Ann Oncol 2003;14:268–272.

2.21.1.8 EVAP

  • Etoposide: 120 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Vinblastine: 4 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Cytarabine: 30 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Cisplatin: 40 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Longo DL. Semin Oncol 1990;17:716–735.

2.21.1.9 Mini-BEAM

  • Carmustine: 60 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Etoposide: 75 mg/m2 IV on days 2–5
  • Ara-C: 100 mg/m2 IV every 12 hours on days 2–5
  • Melphalan: 30 mg/m2 IV on day 6
  • Repeat cycle every 4–6 weeks.

Colwill R, et al. J Clin Oncol 1995;13:396–402.

2.21.1.10 BEACOPP

  • Bleomycin: 10 mg/m2 IV on day 8
  • Etoposide: 100 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Doxorubicin: 25 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cyclophosphamide: 650 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on day 8 (maximum, 2 mg)
  • Procarbazine: 100 mg/m2 PO on days 1–7
  • Prednisone: 40 mg/m2 PO on days 1–14
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Diehl V, et al. J Clin Oncol 1998;16:3810–3821.

2.21.1.11 BEACOPP Escalated

  • Bleomycin: 10 mg/m2 IV on day 8
  • Etoposide: 200 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Doxorubicin: 35 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cyclophosphamide: 1,200 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on day 8 (maximum dose, 2 mg)
  • Procarbazine: 100 mg/m2 PO on days 1–7
  • Prednisone: 40 mg/m2 PO on days 1–14
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days. G-CSF support, at dose of 5 µg/kg/day SC, starting on day 8 and continue until neutrophil recovery.

Tesch H, et al. Blood 1998;15:4560–4567.

2.21.1.12 GVD

For transplant-naïve patients:

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Vinorelbine: 20 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Doxil: 15 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Bartlett NL, et al. Ann Oncol 2007;18:1071–1079.

or For post-transplant patients:

  • Gemcitabine: 800 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Vinorelbine: 15 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Doxil: 10 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Bartlett NL, et al. Ann Oncol 2007;18:1071–1079.

2.21.2 Hodgkin’s Lymphoma - Single-Agent Regimens

2.21.2.1 Gemcitabine

  • Gemcitabine: 1,250 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Santoro A, et al. J Clin Oncol 2000;18:2615–2619.

2.21.2.2 Rituximab

  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat weekly for 4 weeks.

Schulz H, et al. Blood 2008;111:109–111.

2.21.2.3 Brentuximab

  • Brentuximab: 1.8 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 3 weeks for up to 16 cycles.

Younes A, et al. J Clin Oncol 2012;30:2183–2189.

2.21.2.4 Nivolumab

  • Nivolumab: 240 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks. May also administer 480 mg IV with cycles repeated every 4 weeks.

Ansell SM, et al. N Engl J Med 2015;372:311–318.

2.21.2.5 Pembrolizumab

  • Pembrolizumab: 200 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Armand P, et al. J Clin Oncol 2016;34:3733–3739.

2.21.2.6 Bendamustine

  • Bendamustine: 70–120 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 2
  • Repeat weekly for 4 weeks.

Moskowitz AJ, et al. J Clin Oncol 2013;31:456–460.

2.21.2.7 Everolimus

  • Everolimus: 10 mg PO daily
  • Continue until disease progression.

Johnston PB, et al. Am J Hematol 2010;85:320–324.

2.21.2.8 Lenalidomide

  • Lenalidomide: 25 mg PO daily
  • Continue until disease progression.

Fehniger TA, et al. Blood 2011;118:5119–5125.

2.21.3 Non-Hodgkin’s Lymphoma - Low-Grade Lymphoma - Combination Regimens

2.21.3.1 CVP

  • Cyclophosphamide: 400 mg/m2 PO on days 1–5 (or 800 mg/m2 IV on day 1)
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on day 1 (maximum, 2 mg)
  • Prednisone: 100 mg/m2 PO on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Bagley CM Jr, et al. Ann Intern Med 1972;76:227–234.

2.21.3.2 CHOP

  • Cyclophosphamide: 750 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Doxorubicin: 50 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on day 1 (maximum, 2 mg)
  • Prednisone: 100 mg/m2 PO on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Urba WJ, et al. J Natl Cancer Inst Monogr 1990;10:29–37.

2.21.3.3 CNOP

  • Cyclophosphamide: 750 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Mitoxantrone: 10 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on day 1 (maximum, 2 mg)
  • Prednisone: 50 mg/m2 PO on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Sonnevald P, et al. J Clin Oncol 1995;13:2530–2539.

2.21.3.4 FND

  • Fludarabine: 25 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Mitoxantrone: 10 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Dexamethasone: 20 mg PO on days 1–5
  • Trimethoprim/sulfamethoxazole (Bactrim DS): 1 tablet PO bid, 3 times per week
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

McLaughlin P, et al. J Clin Oncol 1996;14:1262–1268.

2.21.3.5 FC

  • Fludarabine: 20 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Cyclophosphamide: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Trimethoprim/sulfamethoxazole (Bactrim DS): 1 tablet PO bid
  • Repeat cycle every 21–28 days.

Hochster H, et al. Blood 1994;84 (Suppl 1):383a.

2.21.3.6 FCR

  • Fludarabine: 25 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Cyclophosphamide: 300 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for 4 cycles.

Sacchi S, et al. Cancer 2007;110:121–128.

2.21.3.7 R-CHOP

  • Cyclophosphamide: 750 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Doxorubicin: 50 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on day 1 (maximum, 2 mg)
  • Prednisone: 100 mg/day PO on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days up to 6 cycles. Patients who experience a response to therapy can then receive maintenance therapy with
  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 3 months up to a maximum of 2 years.

van Oers MHJ, et al. Blood 2006;108:3295–3301.

2.21.3.8 R-FCM

  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 0
  • Fludarabine: 25 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Cyclophosphamide: 200 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Mitoxantrone: 8 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 4 weeks for a total of 4 cycles. Patients who experience a response can then receive maintenance therapy at 3 and 9 months after completion of therapy with
  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV weekly for 4 weeks

Forstpointer R, et al. Blood 2006;108:4003–4008.

2.21.3.9 Bendamustine + Rituximab

  • Bendamustine: 90 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 2
  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for 4 cycles.

Rummel MJ, et al. J Clin Oncol 2005;23:3383–3389.

or

  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Bendamustine: 90 mg/m2 IV on days 2 and 3
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for 4–6 cycles. An additional dose of rituximab is administered 1 week prior to the first cycle and 4 weeks after the last cycle.

Robinson KS, et al. J Clin Oncol 2008;26:4473–4479.

2.21.3.10 Bortezomib (mantle cell lymphoma)

  • Bortezomib: 1.3 mg/m2 IV or SC on days 1, 4, 8, and 11
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for up to 17 cycles.

Fisher RI, et al. J Clin Oncol 2006;24:4867–4874.

2.21.3.11 Ibrutinib (mantle cell lymphoma)

  • Ibrutinib: 560 mg/day PO
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Wang ML, et al. N Engl J Med 2013;369:507–516.

2.21.3.12 Acalabrutinib (mantle cell lymphoma)

  • Acalabrutinib: 100 mg PO bid
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Wang M, et al. Lancet 2018;391:659–667.

2.21.3.13 Copanlisib

  • Copanlisib: 60 mg IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Dreyling M, et al. Ann Oncol 2017;28:2169–2178.

2.21.3.14 Bendamustine + Obinutuzumab

  • Bendamustine: 90 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 2
  • Obinutuzumab: 1,000 mg IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • First cycle is administered over 28 days followed by
  • Bendamustine: 90 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 2
  • Obinutuzumab: 1,000 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for a total of 5 cycles.

Sehn LH, et al. J Clin Oncol 2015;33:LBA8502.

2.21.4 Non-Hodgkin’s Lymphoma - Intermediate-Grade Lymphoma

2.21.4.1 CHOP

  • Cyclophosphamide: 750 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Doxorubicin: 50 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on day 1 (maximum, 2 mg)
  • Prednisone: 100 mg PO on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Klimo P, et al. J Clin Oncol 1985;3:1174–1182.

2.21.4.2 CHOP + Rituximab

  • Cyclophosphamide: 750 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Doxorubicin: 50 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on day 1 (maximum, 2 mg)
  • Prednisone: 40 mg/m2 PO on days 1–5
  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days. Rituximab is to be administered first, followed by cyclophosphamide, doxorubicin, and vincristine.

Coiffier B, et al. N Engl J Med 2002;346:235–242.

or

2.21.4.3 R-CHOP-14

  • Cyclophosphamide: 750 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Doxorubicin: 50 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on day 1 (maximum, 2 mg)
  • Prednisone: 100 mg/day PO on days 1–5
  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks up to 6 cycles. G-CSF support to start on day 4 of each cycle.

Pfreundschuh M, et al. Lancet Oncol 2008;9:105–116.

2.21.4.4 CNOP

  • Cyclophosphamide: 750 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Mitoxantrone: 10 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on day 1 (maximum, 2 mg)
  • Prednisone: 100 mg PO on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Vose JM, et al. Leuk Lymphoma 2002;43:799–804.

2.21.4.5 EPOCH

  • Etoposide: 50 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Prednisone: 60 mg/m2 PO on days 1–5
  • Vincristine: 0.4 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Cyclophosphamide: 750 mg/m2 IV on day 5, begin after infusion
  • Doxorubicin: 10 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Trimethoprim/sulfamethoxazole (Bactrim DS): 1 tablet PO bid, 3 times per week
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Wilson WH, et al. J Clin Oncol 1993;11:1573–1582.

2.21.4.6 EPOCH + Rituximab

  • Etoposide: 50 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Prednisone: 60 mg/m2 PO bid on days 1–5
  • Vincristine: 0.4 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Cyclophosphamide: 750 mg/m2 IV on day 5, begin after infusion
  • Doxorubicin: 10 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days. Rituximab is to be administered first followed by infusions of etoposide, doxorubicin, and vincristine. Prophylaxis with trimethoprim/sulfamethoxazole (Bactrim DS) 1 tablet PO bid, 3 times per week to reduce the risk of Pneumocystis carinii infection.

Wilson WH. Semin Oncol 2000;27 (Suppl 12):30–36.

2.21.4.7 MACOP-B

  • Methotrexate: 400 mg/m2 IV on weeks 2, 6, and 10
  • Leucovorin: 15 mg/m2 PO every 6 hours for 6 doses, beginning 24 hours after methotrexate
  • Doxorubicin: 50 mg/m2 IV on weeks 1, 3, 5, 7, 9, and 11
  • Cyclophosphamide: 350 mg/m2 IV on weeks 1, 3, 5, 7, 9, and 11
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on weeks 2, 4, 6, 8, 10, and 12
  • Prednisone: 75 mg/day PO for 12 weeks with taper over the last 2 weeks
  • Bleomycin: 10 U/m2 IV on weeks 4, 8, and 12
  • Bactrim DS: 1 tablet PO bid
  • Ketoconazole: 200 mg/day PO
  • Administer one cycle.

Klimo P, et al. Ann Intern Med 1985;102:596–602.

2.21.4.8 m-BACOD

  • Methotrexate: 200 mg/m2 IV on days 8 and 15
  • Leucovorin: 10 mg/m2 PO every 6 hours for 8 doses, beginning 24 hours after methotrexate
  • Bleomycin: 4 U/m2 IV on day 1
  • Doxorubicin: 45 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cyclophosphamide: 600 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 1 mg/m2 IV on day 1 (maximum, 2 mg)
  • Dexamethasone: 6 mg/m2 PO on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Shipp MA, et al. Ann Intern Med 1986;104:757–765.

2.21.4.9 ProMACE/CytaBOM

  • Prednisone: 60 mg/m2 PO on days 1–14
  • Doxorubicin: 25 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cyclophosphamide: 650 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Etoposide: 120 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cytarabine: 300 mg/m2 IV on day 8
  • Bleomycin: 5 U/m2 IV on day 8
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on day 8
  • Methotrexate: 120 mg/m2 IV on day 8
  • Leucovorin rescue: 25 mg/m2 PO every 6 hours for 6 doses, beginning 24 hours after methotrexate
  • Trimethoprim/sulfamethoxazole: 1 tablet PO bid on days 1–21
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Longo DL, et al. J Clin Oncol 1991;9:25–38.

2.21.4.10 ESHAP (salvage regimen)

  • Etoposide: 40 mg/m2 IV on days 1–4
  • Methylprednisolone: 500 mg IV on days 1–4
  • Cisplatin: 25 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Cytarabine: 2,000 mg/m2 IV on day 5 after completion of cisplatin and etoposide
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Velasquez WS, et al. J Clin Oncol 1994;12:1169–1176.

2.21.4.11 DHAP (salvage regimen)

  • Cisplatin: 100 mg/m2 IV continuous infusion over 24 hours on day 1
  • Cytarabine: 2,000 mg/m2 IV over 3 hours every 12 hours for 2 doses on day 2 after completion of cisplatin infusion
  • Dexamethasone: 40 mg PO or IV on days 1–4
  • Repeat cycle every 3–4 weeks.

Velasquez WS, et al. Blood 1988;71:117–122.

2.21.4.12 ICE (salvage regimen)

  • Ifosfamide: 5,000 mg/m2 IV continuous infusion for 24 hours on day 2
  • Etoposide: 100 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 5, IV on day 2
  • Mesna: 5,000 mg/m2 IV in combination with ifosfamide dose
  • Repeat cycle every 14 days. G-CSF support is administered at 5 µg/kg/day on days 5–12.

Moskowitz C, et al. J Clin Oncol 1999;17:3776–3785.

2.21.4.13 RICE (salvage regimen)

  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Ifosfamide: 5,000 mg/m2 IV continuous infusion for 24 hours on day 4
  • Etoposide: 100 mg/m2 IV on days 3–5
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 5, IV on day 4
  • Mesna: 5,000 mg/m2 IV in combination with ifosfamide dose
  • Repeat cycle every 14 days. Rituximab is also given at 48 hours before the start of the first cycle. G-CSF is administered at 5 µg/kg/day SC on days 7–14 after the first 2 cycles and at 10 µg/kg/day SC after the third cycle.

Kewairamani T, et al. Blood 2004;103; 3684–3688.

2.21.4.14 MINE (salvage regimen)

  • Mesna: 1,330 mg/m2 IV administered at same time as ifosfamide on days 1–3, then 500 mg IV 4 hours after ifosfamide on days 1–3
  • Ifosfamide: 1,330 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Mitoxantrone: 8 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Etoposide: 65 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Rodriguez MA, et al. Ann Oncol 1995;6:609–611.

2.21.4.15 R-GemOx

  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on day 2
  • Oxaliplatin: 50 mg/m2 IV on day 2
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks for a total of 8 cycles.

El Gnaoui T, et al. Ann Oncol 2007;18:1363–1368.

or

  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 0
  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Oxaliplatin: 100 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks for a total of 6 cycles.

Shen QD, et al. Lancet Hematol 2018. doi:10.1016/S2352-3026 (18)30054-1.

2.21.5 Non-Hodgkin’s Lymphoma - High-Grade Lymphoma

2.21.5.1 Magrath Protocol (Burkitt’s lymphoma)

  • Cyclophosphamide: 1,200 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Doxorubicin: 40 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on day 1 (maximum, 2 mg)
  • Prednisone: 40 mg/m2 PO on days 1–5
  • Methotrexate: 300 mg/m2 IV on day 10 for 1 hour, then 60 mg/m2 IV on days 10 and 11 for 41 hours
  • Leucovorin rescue: 15 mg/m2 IV every 6 hours for 8 doses, starting 24 hours after methotrexate on day 12
  • Intrathecal ara-C: 30 mg/m2 IT on day 7, cycle 1 only; 45 mg/m2 IT on day 7, all subsequent cycles
  • Intrathecal methotrexate: 12.5 mg IT on day 10, all cycles
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Magrath I, et al. Blood 1984;63:1102–1111.

or

2.21.5.2 Regimen A (CODOX-M)

  • Cyclophosphamide: 800 mg/m2 IV on day 1 and 200 mg/m2 IV on days 2–5
  • Doxorubicin: 40 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 1.5 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8 in cycle 1 and on days 1, 8, and 15 in cycle 3
  • Methotrexate: 1,200 mg/m2 IV over 1 hour, followed by 240 mg/m2/hour for the next 23 hours on day 10
  • Leucovorin: 192 mg/m2 IV starting at hour 36 after the start of the infusion and 12 mg/m2 IV every 6 hours thereafter until serum methotrexate levels <50 nM

Magrath I, et al. J Clin Oncol 1996;14:925.

2.21.5.3 CNS Prophylaxis

  • Cytarabine: 70 mg IT on days 1 and 3
  • Methotrexate: 12 mg IT on day 15

2.21.5.4 Regimen B (IVAC)

  • Ifosfamide: 1,500 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Etoposide: 60 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Cytarabine: 2 g/m2 IV every 12 hours on days 1 and 2 for a total of 4 doses
  • Methotrexate: 12 mg IT on day 5

2.21.5.5 Stanford Regimen (small noncleaved cell and Burkitt’s lymphoma)

  • Cyclophosphamide: 1,200 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Doxorubicin: 40 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on day 1 (maximum, 2 mg)
  • Prednisone: 40 mg/m2 PO on days 1–5
  • Methotrexate: 3 g/m2 IV over 6 hours on day 10
  • Leucovorin rescue: 25 mg/m2 IV or PO every 6 hours for 12 doses, beginning 24 hours after methotrexate
  • Intrathecal methotrexate: 12 mg IT on days 1 and 10
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Berstein JI, et al. J Clin Oncol 1986;4:847–858.

2.21.5.6 Hyper-CVAD/Methotrexate-Ara-C

  • Cyclophosphamide: 300 mg/m2 IV every 12 hours for 6 doses on days 1–3
  • Mesna: 600 mg/m2/day continuous infusion on days 1–3 to start 1 hour before cyclophosphamide until 12 hours after completion of cyclophosphamide
  • Vincristine: 2 mg IV on days 4 and 11
  • Doxorubicin: 50 mg/m2 IV over 24 hours on day 4
  • Dexamethasone: 40 mg PO or IV on days 1–4 and days 11–14
  • Administer every 3–4 weeks on cycles 1, 3, 5, and 7.
  • Methotrexate: 200 mg/m2 IV over 2 hours followed by 800 mg/m2 continuous infusion over 22 hours on day 1
  • Cytarabine: 3,000 mg/m2 IV over 2 hours every 12 hours for 4 doses on days 2–3 (1 g/m2 for patients >60 years old)
  • Leucovorin: 50 mg IV every 6 hours starting 12 hours after completion of methotrexate until methotrexate level <50 nM
  • Administer every 3–4 weeks on cycles 2, 4, 6, and 8

Thomas DA, et al. Blood 2004;104:1624–1630.

2.21.5.7 Intrathecal Chemotherapy Prophylaxis

  • Methotrexate: 12 mg IT on day 2 of each cycle for a total of 3–4 treatments
  • Cytarabine: 100 mg IT on day 8 of each cycle for a total of 3–4 treatments
  • Intrathecal Chemotherapy: Administer intrathecal chemotherapy twice a week with methotrexate 12 mg and cytarabine 100 mg, respectively, until no more cancer cells in CSF, then decrease intrathecal chemotherapy to once a week for 4 weeks, followed by methotrexate 12 mg on day 2 and cytarabine 100 mg on day 8 for the remaining chemotherapy cycles.

2.21.5.8 Axicabtagene ciloceucel

  • Cyclophosphamide: 500 mg/m2 IV on days -5, -4, and -3
  • Fludarabine: 30 mg/m2 IV on days -5, -4, and -3
  • Axicabtagene ciloceucel: 2 x 106 CAR-positive T cells/kg body weight IV on day 1

Neelapu SS, et al. N Engl J Med 2017;377:2531–2544.

2.21.5.9 Tisagenlecleucel

  • Cyclophosphamide: 250 mg/m2 IV on days -5, -4, and -3
  • Fludarabine: 25 mg/m2 IV on day -5, -4, and -3
  • Tisagenlecleucel: 0.6–6.0 × 108 CAR-positive T cells/kg body weight IV on day 1

Schuster SJ, et al. N Engl J Med 2017;377:2545–2554.

2.21.6 Non-Hodgkin’s Lymphoma - Single-Agent Regimens

2.21.6.1 Rituximab

  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, 15, and 22
  • Repeat one additional cycle.

McLaughlin P, et al. J Clin Oncol 1998;16:2825–2833.

or

  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, 15, and 22 followed by 375 mg/m2 IV at week 12 and at months 5, 7, and 9.

Ghielmini M, et al. Blood 2004;103:4416–4423.

2.21.6.2 Ibritumomab Tiuxetan Regimen

  • Rituximab: 250 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • 111In-Ibritumomab tiuxetan: 5 mCi of 111In, 1.6 mg of ibritumomab tiuxetan IV on day 1
  • 90Y-Ibritumomab tiuxetan: 0.4 mCi/kg IV over 10 min on day 8 after the day 8 rituximab dose
  • The dose of 90Y-ibritumomab tiuxetan is capped at 32 mCi.

Witzig TE, et al. J Clin Oncol 2002;20:2453–2463.

2.21.6.3 Fludarabine

  • Fludarabine: 25 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Falkson CI. Am J Clin Oncol 1996;19:268–270.

2.21.6.4 Cladribine

  • Cladribine: 0.5–0.7 mg/kg SC on days 1–5 or 0.1 mg/kg IV on days 1–7
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Betticher DC, et al. J Clin Oncol 1998;16:850–858.

2.21.6.5 Bendamustine

  • Bendamustine: 120 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 2
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days up to 8 cycles.

Friedberg JW, et al. J Clin Oncol 2008;26:204–210.

2.21.6.6 Vorinostat (peripheral T-cell lymphoma)

  • Vorinostat: 400 mg PO daily
  • Continue therapy until disease progression. If toxicity is observed, dose may be reduced to 300 mg PO daily.

Mann BS, et al. Oncologist 2007;12:1247–1252.

2.21.6.7 Pralatrexate

  • Pralatrexate: 30 mg/m2 IV weekly for 6 weeks
  • Repeat cycle every 7 weeks. Folic acid at 1–1.25 mg PO q day beginning 10 days prior to therapy and vitamin B12 at 1 mg IM beginning no more than 10 weeks prior to first dose of therapy and repeated every 8–10 weeks.

O’Connor OA, et al. J Clin Oncol 2009;27:4357–4364.

2.21.6.8 Brentuximab

  • Brentuximab: 1.8 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 3 weeks for up to 16 cycles.

Pro B, et al. J Clin Oncol 2012;30:2190–2196.

2.21.6.9 Romidepsin (peripheral T-cell lymphoma)

  • Romidespsin: 14 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Piekarz RI, et al. Blood 2011;117:5827–5834.

2.21.6.10 Belinostat (peripheral T-cell lymphoma)

  • Belinostat: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

O’Connor OA, et al. J Clin Oncol 2015;33:2492–2499.

2.21.6.11 Bortezomib (mantle cell lymphoma)

  • Bortezomib: 1.3–1.5 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 4, 8, and 11
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Strauss SJ, et al. J Clin Oncol 2006;24:2105–2112.

2.21.6.12 Lenalidomide (mantle cell lymphoma)

  • Lenalidomide: 25 mg/day PO on days 1–21
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for up to 52 weeks.

Habermann TM, et al. Br J Haematol 2009;145:344–349.

2.21.6.13 Pembrolizumab

  • Pembrolizumab: 200 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Zinzani PL, et al. Blood 2017;130:267–270.

2.21.7 Primary Cns Lymphoma - Combination Regimens

  • Methotrexate: 3,500 mg/m2 IV over 2 hours every other week for 5 doses
  • Intrathecal methotrexate: 12 mg IT weekly every other week after IV methotrexate
  • Leucovorin: 10 mg IV every 6 hours for 12 doses starting 24 hours after IV methotrexate; 10 mg IV every 12 hours for 8 doses starting 24 hours after IT methotrexate
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 IV every other week along with IV methotrexate
  • Procarbazine: 100 mg/m2/day PO for 7 days on first, third, and fifth cycle of IV methotrexate
  • Once chemotherapy is completed, whole-brain radiation therapy is administered to a total dose of 45 cGy.

Abrey LE, et al. J Clin Oncol 2002;18:3144–3150.

2.21.7.1 R-MPV + Radiation Therapy + Cytarabine

  • Rituximab: 500 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Methotrexate: 3,500 mg/m2 IV on day 2
  • Leucovorin: 20–25 mg every 6 hours starting 24 hours after methotrexate infusion for 72 hours or until serum methotrexate level, 1 × 10-8 mg/dL.
  • Increase leucovorin to 40 mg every 4 hours IV, if methotrexate level > 1 × 10–8 mg/dL at 48 hours or >1 × 10–8 mg/dL at 72 hours
  • Vincristine: 1.4 mg/m2 (maximum, 2.8 mg) IV on day 2
  • Procarbazine: 100 mg/m2 PO on days 1–7 of odd-numbered cycles only
  • If positive CSF cytology, administer 12 mg methotrexate IT between days 5 and 12 of each cycle
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks for 5 cycles.
  • After 5 cycles of R-MPV:
  • If CR, whole-brain radiotherapy (WBRT) 180 cGy/day for 13 days to a total of 2340 cGy beginning 3–5 weeks after the completion of R-MPV.
  • If PR, administer 2 additional cycles of R-MPV. If CR is achieved after 7 cycles of R-MPV, administer WBRT 180 cGy/day × 13 days to a total of 2,340 cGy beginning 3–5 weeks after completion of R-MPV.
  • If persistent disease exists after 7 cycles of R-MPV, administer WBRT 180 cGy/day × 25 days to a total of 4,500 cGy beginning 3–5 weeks after the completion of R-MPV.
  • If stable or progressive disease after 5 cycles of R-MPV, administer WBRT 180 cGy/day for 25 days to a total of 4,500 cGy beginning 3–5 weeks after the completion of R-MPV.
