Three weeks after the completion of WBRT, consolidation therapy is given with cytarabine 3 g/m2/day (maximum, 6 g) IV over 3 hours for 2 days. A second cycle of cytarabine is given 1 month later.

Shah GD, et al. J Clin Oncol 2007;25:4730–4735.

2.21.8 Primary Cns Lymphoma - Single-Agent Regimens

2.21.8.1 High-Dose Methotrexate

  • Methotrexate: 8,000 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks up to 8 cycles, followed by 8,000 mg/m2 IV on day 1 every month up to 100 months.

Batchelor T, et al. J Clin Oncol 2003;21:1044–1049.

2.21.8.2 Temozolomide

  • Temozolomide: 150 mg/m2/day PO on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 4 weeks.

Reni M, et al. Br J Cancer 2007;96:864–867.

2.21.8.3 Topotecan

  • Topotecan: 1.5 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 3 weeks.

Fischer L, et al. Ann Oncol 2006;17:1141–1145.

2.22 MALIGNANT MELANOMA

2.22.1 Adjuvant Therapy - Combination Regimens

2.22.1.1 Dabrafenib + Trametinib

  • Dabrafenib: 150 mg PO bid
  • Trametinib: 2 mg PO daily
  • Continue treatment for up to 12 months.

Hauschild LA, et al. N Engl J Med 2017;377:1813–1823.

2.22.2 Adjuvant Therapy - Single-Agent Regimens

2.22.2.1 Interferon alpha-2b

  • Interferon alpha-2b: 20 million U/m2 IV, 5 times weekly for 4 weeks, then 10 million IU/m2 SC, 3 times weekly for 48 weeks
  • Treatment is for a total of 1 year.

Kirkwood JM, et al. J Clin Oncol 1996;14:7–17.

2.22.2.2 Peg-Interferon alpha-2b

  • Peg-Interferon a-2b: 6 µg/kg SC weekly for 8 weeks, then 3 µg/kg SC weekly for up to 5 years
  • Treatment is for up to a total of 5 years.

Eggermont AM, et al. Lancet 2008;372:117–126.

2.22.2.3 Nivolumab

  • Nivolumab: 240 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks. or
  • Nivolumab: 480 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 4 weeks.

Weber J, et al. N Engl J Med 2017;377:1824–1835.

2.22.2.4 Ipilimumab

  • Ipilimumab: 10 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 3 weeks for 4 doses followed by 10 mg/kg on day 1 every 12 weeks for up to 3 years.

Eggermont AM, et al. Lancet Oncol 2015;16:522–530.

2.22.3 Metastatic Disease - Combination Regimens

2.22.3.1 DTIC + Carmustine + Cisplatin

  • Dacarbazine: 220 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Carmustine: 150 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cisplatin: 25 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Repeat cycle with dacarbazine and cisplatin every 21 days and carmustine every 42 days.

Creagen ET, et al. J Clin Oncol 1999;17:1884–1890.

2.22.3.2 IFN + DTIC

  • Interferon alpha-2b: 15 million IU/m2 IV on days 1–5, 8–12, and 15–19 as induction therapy
  • Interferon alpha-2b: 10 million IU/m2 SC 3 times weekly after induction therapy
  • Dacarbazine: 200 mg/m2 IV on days 22–26
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Falkson CI, et al. J Clin Oncol 1998;16:1743–1751.

2.22.3.3 Temozolomide + Thalidomide

  • Temozolomide: 75 mg/m2/day PO for 6 weeks
  • Thalidomide: 200 mg/day PO for 6 weeks
  • Repeat cycle every 8 weeks. Consider dose escalation to 400 mg/day for patients <70 years and starting at a lower dose of 100 mg/day with dose escalation to 250 mg/day for patient >70 years.

Hwu WJ, et al. J Clin Oncol 2003;21:3351–3356.

2.22.3.4 Dabrafenib + Trametinib

  • Dabrafenib: 150 mg PO bid
  • Trametinib: 2 mg PO daily
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Flaherty KT, et al. N Engl J Med 2012;367:1694–1703

2.22.3.5 Cobimetinib + Vemurafenib

  • Cobimetinib: 60 mg/day PO on days 1–21
  • Vemurafenib: 960 mg PO bid daily
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Larkin J, et al. N Engl J Med 2014;371:1867–1876.

2.22.3.6 Binimetinib + Encorafenib

  • Binimetinib: 45 mg PO bid
  • Encorafenib: 300 mg PO daily
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Dummer R, et al. Lancet Oncol 2018;19:603–615.

2.22.3.7 Nivolumab + Ipilimumab

  • Ipilimumab: 1 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Nivolumab: 1 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for 4 cycles followed by
  • Nivolumab: 240 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 14 days until disease progression.

Larkin J, et al. N Engl J Med 2015;373:23–34.

2.22.4 Metastatic Disease - Single-Agent Regimens

2.22.4.1 Dacarbazine

  • Dacarbazine: 250 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Luce JK, et al. Cancer Chemother Rep 1970;54:119–124.

or

  • Dacarbazine: 850 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 3–6 weeks.

Pritchard KI, et al. Cancer Treat Rep 1980;64:1123–1126.

2.22.4.2 Interferon-alpha

  • Interferon alpha-2b: 20 million IU/m2 IM, 3 times weekly for 12 weeks.

Kirkwood JM, et al. Semin Oncol 1997;24 (Suppl 4):1–48.

2.22.4.3 Aldesleukin

  • Aldesleukin (IL-2): 720,000 IU/kg IV every 8 hours on days 1–5 and 15–19
  • Repeat cycle in 6- to 12-week intervals.

Atkins MB, et al. J Clin Oncol 1999;17:2105–2116.

or

  • Aldesleukin (IL-2): 100,000 IU/kg IV every 4 hours on days 1–5 and 15–19
  • Repeat cycle in 12-week intervals up to a total of 3 cycles.

Parkinson DR, et al. J Clin Oncol 1990;8:1650–1656.

or

  • Aldesleukin (IL-2): 720,000 IU/kg IV at 8 am and 6 pm on days 1–5 and 15–19
  • Treat up to a maximum of 8 total doses on days 1–5 and repeat on days 15–19.
  • Repeat cycle in 8- to 12-week intervals.

Acquavella N, et al. J Immunother 2008;31:569–576.

2.22.4.4 Ipilimumab

  • Ipilimumab: 3 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 3 weeks for a total of 4 doses.

Wolchok JD, et al. Lancet Oncology 2010;11:155–164.

2.22.4.5 Pembrolizumab

  • Pembrolizumab: 200 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 3 weeks.

Robert C, et al. N Engl J Med 2015;372:2521–2532.

2.22.4.6 Nivolumab

  • Nivolumab: 240 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks.

Weber JS, et al. Lancet Oncol 2015;16:375–384.

2.22.4.7 Temozolomide

  • Temozolomide: 150 mg/m2 PO on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days. If tolerated, can increase dose to 200 mg/m2 PO on days 1–5.

Middleton MR, et al. J Clin Oncol 2000;18:158–166.

2.22.4.8 Vemurafenib

  • Vemurafenib: 960 mg PO bid
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Sosman JA, et al. N Engl J Med 2012;366:707–714.

2.22.4.9 Dabrafenib

  • Dabrafenib: 150 mg PO bid
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Falchook GS, et al. Lancet 2012;379:1893–1901.

2.22.4.10 Trametinib

  • Trametinib: 2 mg PO daily
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Kim KB, et al. J Clin Oncol 2013;31:482–489.

2.23 MALIGNANT MESOTHELIOMA

2.23.1 Combination Regimens

2.23.1.1 Doxorubicin + Cisplatin

  • Doxorubicin: 60 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cisplatin: 60 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21–28 days.

Ardizzoni A, et al. Cancer 1991;67:2984–2987.

2.23.1.2 CAP

  • Cyclophosphamide: 500 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Doxorubicin: 50 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cisplatin: 80 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Shin DM, et al. Cancer 1995;76:2230–2236.

2.23.1.3 Gemcitabine + Cisplatin

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Cisplatin: 100 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Nowak AK, et al. Br J Cancer 2002;87:491–496.

2.23.1.4 Gemcitabine + Carboplatin

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 5, IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Favaretto AG, et al. Cancer 2003;97:2791–2797.

2.23.1.5 Pemetrexed + Cisplatin

  • Pemetrexed: 500 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cisplatin: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days. Folic acid at 350–1,000 µg PO q day beginning 1 week prior to therapy and vitamin B12 at 1,000 µg IM to start 1–2 weeks prior to first dose of therapy and repeated every 3 cycles.

Vogelzang NJ, et al. J Clin Oncol 2003;21:2636–2644.

2.23.1.6 Gemcitabine + Vinorelbine

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Vinorelbine: 25 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Zucali PA, et al. Cancer 2008;112:1555–1561.

2.23.1.7 Pemetrexed + Gemcitabine

  • Pemetrexed: 500 mg/m2 IV on day 8
  • Gemcitabine: 1,250 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days. Folic acid at 350–1,000 µg PO q day beginning 1–2 weeks prior to therapy and vitamin B12 at 1,000 µg IM to start 1–2 weeks prior to first dose of therapy and repeated every 3 cycles.

Simon GR, et al. J Clin Oncol 2008;21:3567–3572.

2.23.2 Single-Agent Regimens

2.23.2.1 Pemetrexed

  • Pemetrexed: 500 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days. Folic acid at 350–1,000 µg PO q day beginning 1 week prior to therapy and vitamin B12 at 1,000 µg IM to start 1–2 weeks prior to first dose of therapy and repeated every 3 cycles.
  • Dexamethasone 4 mg PO bid on the day before, day of, and day after each dose of pemetrexed.

Jassem J, et al. J Clin Oncol 2008;26:1698–1704.

2.23.2.2 Vinorelbine

  • Vinorelbine: 30 mg/m2 IV weekly
  • One cycle consists of 6 weekly injections. Continue until disease progression.

Steele JPC, et al. J Clin Oncol 2000;18:3912–3917.

2.23.2.3 Gemcitabine

  • Gemcitabine: 1,250 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days up to a total of 10 cycles.

van Meerbeeck JP, et al. Cancer 1999;85:2577–2582.

2.23.2.4 Pembrolizumab

  • Pembrolizumab: 10 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 14 days.

Alley EW, et al. Lancet Oncol 2017;18:623–630.

2.23.2.5 Nivolumab

  • Nivolumab: 3 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 14 days.

Quispel-Janssen J, et al. J Thorac Oncol 2018. doi: 10.1016/j.jtho.2018.038.

2.24 MERKEL CELL CANCER

2.24.1 Combination Regimens

2.24.1.1 EP

  • Etoposide: 80 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Cisplatin: 80 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Ihde DC, et al. J Clin Oncol 1994;12:2022–2034.

2.24.1.2 EC

  • Etoposide: 100 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Viren M, et al. Acta Oncol 1994;33:921–924

2.24.1.3 CAV

  • Cyclophosphamide: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Doxorubicin: 40 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 1 mg/m2 IV on day 1 (maximum, 2 mg)
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Roth BJ, et al. J Clin Oncol 1992;10:282–291.

2.24.2 Single-Agent Regimens

2.24.2.1 Avelumab

  • Avelumab: 10 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks.

Kaufman HL, et al. Lancet Oncol 2016;10:1374–1385.

2.25 MULTIPLE MYELOMA

2.25.1 Combination Regimens

2.25.1.1 MP

  • Melphalan: 8–10 mg/m2 PO on days 1–4
  • Prednisone: 60 mg/m2 on days 1–4
  • Repeat cycle every 42 days.

Southwest Oncology Group Study. Arch Intern Med 1975;135:147–152.

2.25.1.2 MPT

  • Melphalan: 0.25 mg/kg PO on days 1–4
  • Prednisone: 1.5 mg/kg PO on days 1–4
  • Thalidomide: 50–100 mg/day PO q day
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Palumbo A, et al. Lancet 2006;367:835.

or

  • Melphalan: 0.25 mg/kg/day PO on days 1–4
  • Prednisone: 2 mg/kg/day PO on days 1–4
  • Thalidomide: 100–400 mg PO q day
  • Repeat cycle every 42 days.

Facon T, et al. Proc Am Soc Clin Oncol 2006;24 (abstract 1)

2.25.1.3 MPL

  • Melphalan: 0.18 mg/kg PO on days 1–4
  • Prednisone: 2 mg/kg PO on days 1–4
  • Lenalidomide: 10 mg/day PO on days 1–21
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Palumbo A, et al. J Clin Oncol 2007;25:4459–4465.

2.25.1.4 VAD

  • Vincristine: 0.4 mg/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Doxorubicin: 9 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Dexamethasone: 40 mg PO on days 1–4, 9–12, and 17–20
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Barlogie B, et al. N Engl J Med 1984;310:1353–1356.

2.25.1.5 Thalidomide + Dexamethasone

  • Thalidomide: 200 mg/day PO
  • Dexamethasone: 40 mg/day PO on days 1–4, 9–12, and 17–20 for first 4 cycles and then 40 mg/day PO on days 1–4
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Rajkumar SV, et al. J Clin Oncol 2002;20:4319–4323.

2.25.1.6 Lenalidomide + Dexamethasone

  • Lenalidomide: 25 mg/day PO on days 1–21
  • Dexamethasone: 40 mg/day PO on days 1–4, 9–12, and 17–20 (first 4 cycles) and then 40 mg/day PO on days 1–4 with future cycles
  • Repeat cycles every 28 days.

Richardson PG, et al. Blood 2006;108:3458–3464.

or

  • Lenalidomide: 25 mg/day PO on days 1–21
  • Dexamethasone: 40 mg/m2/day PO on days 1, 8, 15, and 22
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Rajkumar SV, et al. Proc Am Soc Clin Oncol 2007;25 (LBA8025).

2.25.1.7 RVD

  • Lenalidomide: 25 mg/day PO on days 1–14
  • Bortezomib: 1.3 mg/m2 IV or SC on days 1, 4, 8, and 11
  • Dexamethasone: 20 mg/day PO on days 1, 2, 4, 5, 8, 9, 11, and 12
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for 8 cycles.

Richardson PG, et al. Blood 2010;116:679–686.

2.25.1.8 Panobinostat + Bortezomib + Dexamethasone

  • Panobinostat: 20 mg/day PO on days 1, 3, 5, 8, 10, and 12
  • Bortezomib: 1.3 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 4, 8, and 11
  • Dexamethasone: 20 mg/day PO on days 1, 2, 4, 5, 8, 9, 11, and 12
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

San-Miguel JF, et al. Lancet Oncol 2014;15:1195–1206.

2.25.1.9 PD

  • Pomalidomide: 4 mg/day PO on days 1–21
  • Dexamethasone: 40 mg/day PO on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Leleu X, et al. Blood 2013;121:1968–1975.

or

  • Pomalidomide: 2 mg/day PO on days 1–21
  • Dexamethasone: 40 mg/day PO on days 1, 8, 15, and 22
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Lacy MQ, et al. Blood 2009;27:5008–5014.

2.25.1.10 DVD

  • Doxorubicin liposome: 40 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 2 mg IV on day 1
  • Dexamethasone: 40 mg PO on days 1–4
  • Repeat cycles every 28 days.

Hussein MA, et al. Cancer 2002;95:2160–2168.

2.25.1.11 Bortezomib + Doxorubicin liposome

  • Bortezomib: 1.3 mg/m2 IV or SC on days 1, 4, 8, and 11
  • Doxorubicin liposome: 30 mg/m2 IV infusion on day 4
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Orlowski RZ, et al. Proc Am Soc Hematol 2006 (abstract 404).

2.25.1.12 Bortezomib + Melphalan

  • Bortezomib: 1.0 mg/m2 IV or SC on days 1, 4, 8, and 11
  • Melphalan: 0.10 mg/kg PO on days 1–4
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days up to 8 cycles.

Berenson JR, et al. J Clin Oncol 2006;24:937–944.

2.25.1.13 BMP

  • Bortezomib: 1.3 mg/m2 IV or SC on days 1, 4, 8, 11, 22, 25, 29, and 32
  • Melphalan: 9 mg/m2 PO on days 1–4
  • Prednisone: 60 mg/m2 PO on days 1–4
  • Repeat cycle every 6 weeks for 4 cycles, then
  • Bortezomib: 1.3 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, 22, and 29
  • Melphalan: 9 mg/m2 PO on days 1–4
  • Prednisone: 60 mg/m2 PO on days 1–4
  • Repeat cycle every 6 weeks for 5 cycles.

San Miguel JF, et al. N Engl J Med 2008;359:906–917.

2.25.1.14 BMPT

  • Bortezomib: 1–1.3 mg/m2 IV or SC on days 1, 4, 15, and 22
  • Melphalan: 6 mg/m2 PO on days 1–5
  • Prednisone: 60 mg/m2 PO on days 1–5
  • Thalidomide: 50 mg PO daily
  • Repeat cycle every 5 weeks for 6 cycles.

Palumbo A, et al. Blood 2007;109:2757–2762.

2.25.1.15 RMPT

  • Lenalidomide: 10 mg PO on days 1–21
  • Melphalan: 0.18 mg/kg PO on days 1–4
  • Prednisone: 2 mg/kg PO on days 1–4
  • Thalidomide: 50 mg PO daily on days 1–28
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for 6 cycles followed by maintenance lenalidomide 10 mg PO on days 1–21 until progression or toxicity.

Palumbo A, et al. Leukemia 2010;24:1037–1042.

2.25.1.16 Carfilzomib + Lenalidomide + Dexamethasone (CLD)

  • Carfilzomib: 20 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 2 of cycle 1, and if tolerated, then 27 mg/m2 IV on days 8, 9, 15, and 16 during cycles 1 through 12 and 27 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 2, 15, and 16 during cycles 13 through 18 after which carfilzomib is discontinued
  • Lenalidomide: 25 mg PO on days 1–21
  • Dexamethasone: 40 mg PO on days 1, 8, 15, and 22
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for up to 9 cycles.

Stewart AK, et al. N Engl J Med 2015;372:142–152.

2.25.1.17 Carfilzomib + Dexamethasone (CD)

  • Carfilzomib: 20 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15 of cycle 1, and then 70 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15 for all subsequent cycles
  • Dexamethasone: 40 mg PO on days 1, 8, and 15 for all cycles 40 mg PO on days 1, 8, 15, and 22 (cycles 1–9 only)
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Moreau P, et al. Lancet Oncol 2018;dx. doi.org/10.1016/S1470-2045(18)30354-1.

2.25.1.18 Lenalidomide + Dexamethasone + Ixazomib

  • Lenalidomide: 25 mg/day PO on days 1–21
  • Dexamethasone: 40 mg/day PO on days 1, 8, 15, and 22
  • Ixazomib: 4 mg/day PO on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days until disease progression.

Moreau P, et al. Blood 2015;126:727.

2.25.1.19 Daratumumab + Bortezomib + Dexamethasone

  • Daratumumab: 16 mg/kg IV weekly on cycles 1–3, 16 mg/kg IV on day 1 of cycles 4–8, 16 mg/kg IV on day 1 of cycles 9+
  • Bortezomib: 1.3 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 4, 8, and 11 on cycles 1–8
  • Dexamethasone: 20 mg PO on days 1, 2, 4, 5, 8, 9, 11, and 12 on cycles 1–8
  • Continue treatment until disease progression or toxicity.

Lokhorst HM, et al. N Engl J Med 2015;373:1207–1219.

2.25.1.20 Elotuzumab + Lenalidomide + Dexamethasone

  • Elotuzumab: 10 mg/kg IV on days 1, 8, 15, and 22
  • Lenalidomide: 25 mg PO on days 1–21
  • Dexamethasone: 8 mg IV prior to elotuzumab infusion and 28 mg PO on days 1, 8, 15, and 22 and 40 mg PO on day 28
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for two cycles followed by:
  • Elotuzumab: 10 mg/kg IV on days 1 and 15
  • Lenalidomide: 25 mg PO on days 1–21
  • Dexamethasone: 8 mg IV prior to elotuzumab infusion and 28 mg PO on days 1 and 15, and 40 mg PO on days 22 and 28
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days until disease progression.

Lonial S, et al. N Engl J Med 2015;373:621–631.

2.25.2 Single-Agent Regimens

2.25.2.1 Dexamethasone

  • Dexamethasone: 40 mg IV or PO on days 1–4, 9–12, and 17–20
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Alexanian R, et al. Ann Intern Med 1986;105:8–11.

2.25.2.2 Melphalan

  • Melphalan: 90–140 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28–42 days.

Cunningham D, et al. J Clin Oncol 1994;12:764–768.

2.25.2.3 Thalidomide

  • Thalidomide: 200–800 mg PO daily
  • Continue treatment until disease progression or undue toxicity.

Singhal S, et al. N Engl J Med 1999;341:1565–1571.

2.25.2.4 Lenalidomide

  • Lenalidomide: 30 mg PO daily on days 1–21
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days until disease progression or undue toxicity.

Richardson PG, et al. Blood 2006;108:3458–3464.

or

2.25.2.5 Lenalidomide

  • Lenalidomide: 10 mg PO daily on days 1–21
  • For maintenance therapy after autologous stem-cell transplantation, repeat cycle every 28 days until disease progression or undue toxicity.

Palumbo A, et al. N Engl J Med 2014;371:895–905.

2.25.2.6 Bortezomib

  • Bortezomib: 1.3 mg/m2 IV or SC on days 1, 4, 8, and 11
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Richardson P, et al. N Engl J Med 2003;348:2609–2617.

2.25.2.7 Carfilzomib

  • Carfilzomib: 20 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 2, 8, 9, 15, and 16. After cycle 1, increase dose to 27 mg/m2 IV
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for up to 12 cycles.

Vij R, et al. Blood 2012;119:5661–5670.

2.25.2.8 Daratumumab

  • Daratumumab: 16 mg/kg IV on days 1, 8, 15, 22, 29, 36, 42, and 49; followed by once every 2 weeks for 16 weeks; followed by once every 4 weeks
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Lonial S, et al. Lancet 2016;387:1551–1560.

2.25.2.9 Ibrutinib

  • Ibrutinib: 420 mg/day PO daily
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Treon SP, et al. N Engl J Med 2015;372:1430–1400.

2.26 MYELODYSPLASTIC SYNDROME

2.26.1 Single-Agent Regimens

2.26.1.1 Azacitidine

  • Azacitidine: 75 mg/m2 SC daily for 7 days
  • Repeat cycle every 4 weeks. Patients should be treated for at least 4 cycles.

Silverman LR, et al. J Clin Oncol 2006;24:3895–3903.

2.26.1.2 Decitabine

  • Decitabine: 15 mg/m2 IV continuous infusion over 3 hours every 8 hours for 3 days
  • Repeat cycle every 4 weeks. Patients should be treated for at least 4 cycles.

Kantarjian HM, et al. Cancer 2006;106:1794–1803.

or

  • Decitabine: 20 mg/m2 IV continuous infusion over 1 hour for 5 days
  • Repeat cycle every 4–6 weeks. Patients should be treated for at least 4 cycles.

Kantarjian HM, et al. Semin Hematology 2005;32 (Suppl 2): S17–S22.

2.26.1.3 Lenalidomide

  • Lenalidomide: 10 mg PO daily
  • Continue until disease progression.

or

  • Lenalidomide: 10 mg PO daily for 21 days
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Galili N, et al. Expert Opin Investig Drugs 2006;15:805–813.

2.26.1.4 Imatinib

  • Imatinib: 400 mg PO daily
  • Continue until disease progression.

David M, et al. Blood 2007;109:61–64.

2.26.1.5 Antithymocyte globulin (ATG) + Cyclosporine

  • ATG: 15 mg/kg IV on days 1–5
  • Cyclosporine: 5–6 mg/kg PO bid
  • Adjust cyclosporine dose to maintain blood levels between 100 and 300 ng/mL.

Passweg JR, et al. J Clin Oncol 2011;29:303–309.

2.27 OSTEOGENIC SARCOMA

2.27.1 Combination Regimens

2.27.1.1 Etoposide + Ifosfamide

  • Etoposide: 100 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–5
  • Ifosfamide: 3,500 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–5
  • Mesna: 700 mg/m2 IV with first ifosfamide dose, then 3, 6, and 9 hours later on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for 2 cycles. Start G-CSF support at 5 µg/kg/day SC to start on day 6. Followed by surgical resection of primary tumor and then intensive maintenance chemotherapy.
  • Methotrexate: 1,200 mg/m2 IV on weeks 1, 2, 6, 7, 11, 12, 16, 17, 30, and 31
  • Leucovorin: 15 mg IV every 6 hours for 10 doses starting 24 hours after start of highdose methotrexate or
  • L-Leucovorin: 7.5 mg IV every 6 hours for 10 doses starting 24 hours after start of highdose methotrexate
  • Doxorubicin: 37.5 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–2 on weeks 3, 13, 21, 27, and 32
  • Cisplatin: 60 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–2 on weeks 3, 13, 21, and 27
  • Ifosfamide: 2,400 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–5 on weeks 8, 18, and 24
  • Administer G-CSF support at 5 µg/kg/day SC on weeks 8, 18, and 24.

Goorin A, et al. Med Pediatr Oncol 1995;24:362–367.

2.27.1.2 Cisplatin + Doxorubicin + High-Dose Methotrexate

  • Doxorubicin: 25 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–3 on weeks 0 and 5
  • Cisplatin: 120 mg/m2 IV on day 1 on weeks 0 and 5
  • Methotrexate: 1,200 mg/m2 IV on day 1 on weeks 3, 4, 8, and 9
  • Leucovorin: 10 mg IV every 6 hours for 10 doses starting 24 hours after start of highdose methotrexate or
  • L-Leucovorin: 7.5 mg IV every 6 hours for 10 doses starting 24 hours after start of highdose methotrexate
  • Induction chemotherapy is followed by surgical resection of primary tumor and then maintenance chemotherapy to begin on week 12 and continuing until week 31.
  • Doxorubicin: 25 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–3 on weeks 12, 17, 22, and 27
  • Cisplatin: 120 mg/m2 IV on day 1 on weeks 12 and 17
  • Methotrexate: 1,200 mg/m2 IV on day 1 on weeks 15, 16, 20, 21, 25, 26, 30, and 31
  • Leucovorin: 10 mg IV every 6 hours for 10 doses starting 24 hours after start of highdose methotrexate or L-Leucovorin: 7.5 mg IV every 6 hours for 10 doses starting 24 hours after start of highdose methotrexate

Meyers PA, et al. J Clin Oncol 2005;23:2004–2011.

2.28 OVARIAN CANCER (EPITHELIAL)

2.28.1 Combination Regimens

2.28.1.1 CC

  • Carboplatin: 300 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cyclophosphamide: 600 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Swenerton K, et al. J Clin Oncol 1992;10:718–726.

2.28.1.2 CC

  • Cisplatin: 100 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cyclophosphamide: 600 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Alberts D, et al. J Clin Oncol 1992;10:706–717.

2.28.1.3 CP

  • Cisplatin: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 2
  • Paclitaxel: 135 mg/m2 IV over 24 hours on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

McGuire WP, et al. N Engl J Med 1996;334:1–6.

2.28.1.4 Carboplatin + Paclitaxel

  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6–7.5, IV on day 1
  • Paclitaxel: 175 mg/m2 IV over 3 hours on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Ozols RE. Semin Oncol 1995;22 (Suppl 15):1–6.

or

  • Carboplatin: AUC of 2, IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Paclitaxel: 60 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Pignata S, et al. Crit Rev Oncol Hematol 2008;66:229–236.

2.28.1.5 Carboplatin + Paclitaxel + Bevacizumab

  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Paclitaxel: 175 mg/m2 IV over 3 hours on day 1
  • Bevacizumab: 15 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for 6 cycles, then maintenance bevacizumab for cycles 7–22.

Burger RA, et al. J Clin Oncol 2010:28:946S (LBA1).

2.28.1.6 Carboplatin + Docetaxel

  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Docetaxel: 60 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Markman M, et al. J Clin Oncol 2001;19:1901–1905.

2.28.1.7 Carboplatin + Doxorubicin liposome

  • Carboplatin: AUC of 5, IV on day 1
  • Doxorubicin liposome: 30 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Pignant S, et al. J Clin Oncol 2009;27:18S (LBA5509).

2.28.1.8 Gemcitabine + Doxorubicin liposome

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Doxorubicin liposome: 30 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

D’Agostino G, et al. Br J Cancer 2003;89:1180–1184.

2.28.1.9 Gemcitabine + Cisplatin

  • Gemcitabine: 800–1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Cisplatin: 30 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Nagourney RA, et al. Gynecol Oncol 2003;88:35–39.

2.28.1.10 Gemcitabine + Carboplatin

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 4, IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Thigpen T. Semin Oncol 2006;33 (Suppl 6):S26–S32.

2.28.1.11 Paclitaxel + IP Cisplatin + IP Paclitaxel

  • Paclitaxel: 135 mg/m2 IV over 24 hours on day 1
  • Cisplatin: 100 mg/m2 IP on day 2
  • Paclitaxel: 60 mg/m2 IP on day 8
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days up to 6 cycles.

Armstrong DK, et al. N Engl J Med 2006;354:34–43.

2.28.1.12 Pemetrexed + Carboplatin

  • Pemetrexed: 500 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Carboplatin: AUC of 5, IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days. Folic acid at 350–1,000 µg PO q day beginning 1–2 weeks prior to therapy and vitamin B12 at 1,000 µg IM to start 1–2 weeks prior to first dose of therapy and repeated every 3 cycles. Dexamethasone 4 mg PO bid on the day before, day of, and day after each dose of pemetrexed.

Matulonis UA, et al. J Clin Oncol 2008;26:5761–5766.

2.28.2 Single-Agent Regimens

2.28.2.1 Altretamine

  • Altretamine: 260 mg/m2/day PO in 4 divided doses after meals and at bedtime
  • Repeat cycle every 14–21 days.

Markman M. Gynecol Oncol 1998;69:226–229.

2.28.2.2 Doxorubicin liposome

  • Doxorubicin liposome: 40–50 mg/m2 IV over 1 hour on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Rose PG, et al. Gynecol Oncol 2001;82:323–328.

2.28.2.3 Paclitaxel

  • Paclitaxel: 135 mg/m2 IV over 3 hours on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

McGuire WP, et al. Ann Intern Med 1989;111:273–279.

2.28.2.4 Ixabepilone

  • Ixabepilone: 20 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

DeGeest K, et al. J Clin Oncol 2010:28:149–153.

2.28.2.5 Topotecan

  • Topotecan: 1.5 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Kudelka AP, et al. J Clin Oncol 1996;14:1552–1557.

2.28.2.6 Gemcitabine

  • Gemcitabine: 800 mg/m2 IV weekly for 3 weeks
  • Repeat cycle every 4 weeks.

Lund B, et al. J Natl Cancer Inst 1994;86:1530–1533.

2.28.2.7 Etoposide

  • Etoposide: 50 mg/m2/day PO on days 1–21
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Ozols RF. Drugs 1999;58 (Suppl 3):43–49.

2.28.2.8 Vinorelbine

  • Vinorelbine: 30 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Sorensen P, et al. Gynecol Oncol 2001;81:58–62.

2.28.2.9 Pemetrexed

  • Pemetrexed: 900 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days. Folic acid at 350–1,000 µg PO q day beginning 1 week prior to therapy and vitamin B12 at 1,000 µg IM to start 1–2 weeks prior to first dose of therapy and repeated every 3 cycles. Dexamethasone 4 mg PO bid on the day before, day of, and day after each dose of pemetrexed.

Miller DS, et al. J Clin Oncol 2009;27:2686–2691.

2.28.2.10 Bevacizumab

  • Bevacizumab: 15 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Burger RA, et al. J Clin Oncol 2007;25:5165–5171.

2.28.2.11 Capecitabine

  • Capecitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 PO bid on days 1–14
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Wolf JK, et al. Gynecol Oncol 2006;102:468–474.

2.28.2.12 Olaparib

  • Olaparib: 400 PO bid
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Ledermann J, et al. Lancet Oncol 2014;15:852–861.

2.28.2.13 Rucaparib

  • Rucaparib: 600 PO daily
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Swisher E, et al. Lancet Oncol 2017;18:75–87.

2.28.2.14 Niraparib

  • Niraparib: 300 PO daily
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Mirza M, et al. N Engl J Med 2016;375:2154–2164.

2.29 OVARIAN CANCER (GERM CELL)

2.29.1 Combination Regimens

2.29.1.1 BEP

  • Bleomycin: 30 U IV on days 2, 9, and 16
  • Etoposide: 100 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Cisplatin: 20 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Dimopoulos MA, et al. Gynecol Oncol 2004;95:695–700.

2.30 PANCREATIC CANCER

2.30.1 Adjuvant Therapy - Combination Regimens

2.30.1.1 Gemcitabine + Capecitabine (GEM-CAP)

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Capecitabine: 880 mg/m2 PO bid on days 1–21
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for a total of 6 cycles.

Neoptolemos JP, et al. Lancet 2017;389:1011–1024.

2.30.1.2 FOLFIRINOX

  • Oxaliplatin: 85 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Irinotecan: 150 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Leucovorin: 400 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • 5-Fluorouracil: 2,400 mg/m2 IV continuous infusion over 46 hours on days 1 and 2
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks for a total of 12 cycles.

Conroy T, et al. J Clin Oncol 2018;36:18S (abstract LBA4001).

2.30.2 Adjuvant Therapy - Single-Agent Regimens

2.30.2.1 5-Fluorouracil + Leucovorin

  • 5-Fluorouracil: 425 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Leucovorin: 20 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for a total of 6 cycles.

Neoptolemos J, et al. J Clin Oncol 2009;27:18S (abstract LBA4505).

2.30.2.2 Gemcitabine

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for a total of 6 cycles.

Oettle H, et al. JAMA 2007;297:267–277.

2.30.3 Locally Advanced Disease - Combination Regimens

2.30.3.1 5-Fluorouracil + Radiation Therapy (GITSG regimen)

  • 5-Fluorouracil: 500 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–3 and 29–31, then weekly beginning on day 71
  • Radiation therapy: Total dose, 4,000 cGy
  • Chemotherapy and radiation therapy started on the same day and given concurrently.

Gastrointestinal Tumor Study Group. Int J Radiat Oncol Biol Phys 1979;5:1643–1647.

2.30.3.2 RTOG Chemoradiation Regimen

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Followed by concurrent chemoradiation:
  • 5-Fluorouracil: 250 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion during radiation therapy
  • Radiation therapy: 180 cGy/day to a total dose of 5,040 cGy
  • Chemotherapy and radiation therapy started on the same day and given concurrently.
  • After chemoradiation:
  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 4 weeks for a total of 3 cycles.

Regine WF, et al. J Clin Oncol 2006;25 (abstract 4007).

2.30.3.3 Gemcitabine + Radiation Therapy (ECOG regimen)

  • Gemcitabine: 600 mg/m2 IV weekly for 6 weeks
  • Radiation therapy: 180 cGy/day to a total dose of 5,040 cGy. Chemotherapy and radiation therapy started on the same day and given concurrently.
  • Four weeks after the completion of chemoradiation:
  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 4 weeks for a total of 5 cycles.

Loehrer PJ, et al. J Clin Oncol 2008;26 (abstract 4506).

2.30.4 Metastatic Disease - Combination Regimens

2.30.4.1 5-Fluorouracil + Leucovorin

  • 5-Fluorouracil: 425 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Leucovorin: 20 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

DeCaprio JA, et al. J Clin Oncol 1991;9:2128–2133.

2.30.4.2 Gemcitabine + Capecitabine (GEM-CAP)

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Capecitabine: 650 mg/m2 PO bid on days 1–14
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Hess V, et al. J Clin Oncol 2003;21:66–68.

or

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Capecitabine: 830 mg/m2 PO bid on days 1–21
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Hubner RA, et al. Pancreas 2013;42:511–515.

2.30.4.3 Gemcitabine + Docetaxel + Capecitabine (GTX)

  • Gemcitabine: 750 mg/m2 IV over 75 minutes on days 4 and 11
  • Docetaxel: 30 mg/m2 IV on days 4 and 11
  • Capecitabine: 750 mg/m2 PO bid on days 1–14
  • Repeat cycle every 3 weeks.

Fine RL, et al. Cancer Chemother Pharmacol 2008;61:167–175.

2.30.4.4 Gemcitabine + Oxaliplatin

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV over 100 minutes on day 1
  • Oxaliplatin: 100 mg/m2 over 2 hours on day 2
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks.

Louvet C, et al. J Clin Oncol 2002;20:1512–1518.

or

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV over 100 minutes on day 1
  • Oxaliplatin: 100 mg/m2 over 2 hours on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks.

Louvet C, et al. J Clin Oncol 2007;25:18S (abstract 4592).

2.30.4.5 Gemcitabine + Erlotinib

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV weekly for 7 weeks, then 1-week rest; subsequent cycles 1,000 mg/m2 IV weekly for 3 weeks with 1-week rest
  • Erlotinib: 100 mg PO daily
  • Repeat 3-week cycles every 28 days.

Moore MJ, et al. J Clin Oncol 2005;23:16S (abstract 1).

2.30.4.6 Capecitabine + Erlotinib

  • Capecitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 PO bid on days 1–14
  • Erlotinib: 150 mg PO daily
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Kulke MH, et al. J Clin Oncol 2007;25:4787–4792.

2.30.4.7 FOLFIRINOX

  • Oxaliplatin: 85 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Irinotecan: 180 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Leucovorin: 400 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • 5-Fluorouracil: 400 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • 5-Fluorouracil: 2,400 mg/m2 IV continuous infusion over 46 hours on days 1 and 2
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks.

Conroy T, et al. J Clin Oncol 2010;28:302S (abstract 4010).

2.30.4.8 Nab-Paclitaxel + Gemcitabine

  • Nab-Paclitaxel: 125 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Von Hoff DD, et al. N Engl J Med 2013;369:1691–1703.

2.30.4.9 Liposomal Irinotecan + 5-Fluorouracil + Leucovorin

  • Liposomal Irinotecan: 70 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • 5-Fluorouracil: 2,400 mg/m2 IV continuous infusion over 46 hours on days 1 and 2
  • Leucovorin: 400 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks.

Wang-Gilam A, et al. Lancet 2016;387:545–557.

2.30.5 Metastatic Disease - Single-Agent Regimens

2.30.5.1 Gemcitabine

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV weekly for 7 weeks, then 1-week rest; subsequent cycles 1,000 mg/m2 IV weekly for 3 weeks with 1-week rest
  • Repeat 3-week cycle every 28 days.

Burris HA, et al. J Clin Oncol 1997;15:2403–2413.

or

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV over 100 min at 10 mg/m2/min on days 1, 8, and 5
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Brand R, et al. Invest New Drugs 1997;15:331–341.

2.30.5.2 Capecitabine

  • Capecitabine: 1,250 mg/m2 PO bid on days 1–14
  • May decrease dose to 850–1,000 mg/m2 PO bid on days 1–14 to reduce the risk of toxicity without compromising clinical efficacy.
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Cartwright TH, et al. J Clin Oncol 2002;20:160–164.

2.31 PROSTATE CANCER

2.31.1 Combination Regimens

2.31.1.1 Flutamide + Leuprolide

  • Flutamide: 250 mg PO tid
  • Leuprolide: 7.5 mg IM every 28 days or 22.5 mg IM every 12 weeks

Eisenberger MA, et al. Semin Oncol 1994;21:613–619.

2.31.1.2 Flutamide + Goserelin

  • Flutamide: 250 mg PO tid
  • Goserelin: 10.8 mg SC every 12 weeks

Jurincic CD, et al. Semin Oncol 1991;18 (Suppl 6):21–25.

2.31.1.3 Estramustine + Etoposide

  • Estramustine: 15 mg/kg/day PO in 4 divided doses on days 1–21
  • Etoposide: 50 mg/m2/day PO in 2 divided doses on days 1–21
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Pienta KJ, et al. J Clin Oncol 1994;12:2005–2012.

2.31.1.4 Estramustine + Vinblastine

  • Estramustine: 600 mg/m2 PO daily on days 1–42
  • Vinblastine: 4 mg/m2 IV weekly for 6 weeks
  • Repeat cycle every 8 weeks.

Hudes GR, et al. J Clin Oncol 1992;11:1754–1761.

2.31.1.5 Paclitaxel + Estramustine

  • Paclitaxel: 120 mg/m2 IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Estramustine: 600 mg/m2 PO daily, starting 24 hours before paclitaxel
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Hudes GR, et al. J Clin Oncol 1997;15:3156–3163.

or

  • Paclitaxel: 90 mg/m2 IV weekly for 3 weeks
  • Estramustine: 140 mg PO tid, starting day before, day of, and day after paclitaxel
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Vaughn DJ, et al. Cancer 2004;100:746–750.

2.31.1.6 Mitoxantrone + Prednisone

  • Mitoxantrone: 12 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Prednisone: 5 mg PO bid daily
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Tannock IF, et al. J Clin Oncol 1996;14:1756–1764.

2.31.1.7 Docetaxel + Estramustine

  • Docetaxel: 35 mg/m2 IV on day 2 of weeks 1 and 2
  • Estramustine: 420 mg PO for the first 4 doses and 280 mg PO for the next 5 doses on days 1–3 of weeks 1 and 2
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days. Dexamethasone is administered at 4 mg PO bid on days 1–3 of weeks 1 and 2.

Copur MS, et al. Semin Oncol 2001;28:16–21.

or

  • Docetaxel: 60 mg/m2 IV on day 2
  • Estramustine: 280 mg PO tid on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Petrylak DP, et al. N Engl J Med 2004;351:1513–1520.

2.31.1.8 Docetaxel + Prednisone

  • Docetaxel: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Prednisone: 5 mg PO bid
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for up to a total of 10 cycles.

Tannock IF, et al. N Engl J Med 2004;351:1502–1512.

2.31.1.9 Docetaxel + Prednisone + Bevacizumab

  • Docetaxel: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Prednisone: 5 mg PO bid
  • Bevacizumab: 15 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Halabi S, et al. J Clin Oncol 2010;28:951S (LBA 4511).

2.31.1.10 Cabazitaxel + Prednisone

  • Cabazitaxel: 25 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Prednisone: 10 mg PO daily
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

DeBono JS, et al. J Clin Oncol 2010;28:344S (abstract 4508).

or

  • Cabazitaxel: 20 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Prednisone: 10 mg PO daily
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Eisenberger M, et al. J Clin Oncol 2017;35:3198–3206.

or

  • Cabazitaxel: 10 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, 15, and 22
  • Prednisone: 5 mg PO bid
  • Repeat cycle every 5 weeks.

Climent MA, et al. Eur J Cancer 2017;878:30–37.

2.31.1.11 Abiraterone + Prednisone

  • Abiraterone: 1,000 mg PO daily
  • Prednisone: 5 mg PO bid
  • Continue until disease progression.

DeBono JS, et al. N Engl J Med 2011;364:1995–2005.

2.31.1.12 Docetaxel + Leuprolide

  • Docetaxel: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1 every 28 days
  • Leuprolide: 7.5 mg IM on day 1 every 21 days
  • Continue until disease progression.

Sweeney C, et al. J Clin Oncol 2014;32:5S (LBA2).

2.31.2 Single-Agent Regimens

2.31.2.1 Paclitaxel

  • Paclitaxel: 135–170 mg/m2 IV as a 24-hour infusion on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 3 weeks.

Roth BJ, et al. Cancer 1993;72:2457–2460.

or

  • Paclitaxel: 150 mg/m2 IV as a 1-hour infusion weekly for 6 weeks
  • Repeat cycle every 8 weeks.

Ahmed S, et al. Proc Am Soc Clin Oncol 1998;17:325a.

2.31.2.2 Docetaxel

  • Docetaxel: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Petrylak DP. Semin Oncol 2000;27 (Suppl 3):24–29.

or

  • Docetaxel: 20–40 mg/m2 weekly for 3 weeks
  • Repeat cycle every 4 weeks.

Dreicer R. Hematol Oncol Clin North Am 2006;20:935–946.

2.31.2.3 Estramustine

  • Estramustine: 14 mg/kg/day PO in 3–4 divided doses.

Neoptolemos JP, et al. Lancet 2017;389:1011–1024.

2.31.2.4 Goserelin

  • Goserelin: 3.6 mg SC on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Murphy GP, et al. Urology 1984;23:54–63.

or

  • Goserelin: 10.8 mg SC on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 12 weeks.

Dijkman GA, et al. Eur Urol 1995;27:43–46.

2.31.2.5 Goserelin (adjuvant therapy)

  • Goserelin: 3.6 mg SC on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for 24 months.

Hanks GE, et al. J Clin Oncol 2003;21:3972–3978.

2.31.2.6 Degarelix

  • Degarelix: 240 mg SC starting dose followed 28 days later by the first maintenance dose of 80 mg SC
  • Repeat maintenance dose every 28 days.

Klotz L, et al. BJU Int 2008;10:1531–1538.

2.31.2.7 Leuprolide

  • Leuprolide: 7.5 mg SC on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

The Leuprolide Study Group. N Engl J Med 1984;311:1281–1286.

or

  • Leuprolide: 22.5 mg SC on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 12 weeks.

Sharifi R, et al. Clin Ther 1996;18:647–657.

or

  • Leuprolide: 30 mg SC on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 16 weeks.

Sartor O, et al. Urology 2003;62:319–323.

2.31.2.8 Bicalutamide

  • Bicalutamide: 50 mg PO daily.

In patients refractory to other anti-androgen agents, may start with a higher dose of 150 mg PO daily.

Schellhammer PF, et al. Urology 1997;50:330–336.

2.31.2.9 Flutamide

  • Flutamide: 250 mg PO tid.

McLeod DG, et al. Cancer 1993;72:3870–3873.

2.31.2.10 Nilutamide

  • Nilutamide: 300 mg PO on days 1–30, then 150 mg PO daily.

Janknegt RA, et al. J Urol 1993;149:77–82.

2.31.2.11 Apalutamide

  • Apalutamide: 240 mg PO daily.

Smith MR, et al. N Engl J Med 2018;378:1408–1418.

2.31.2.12 Prednisone

  • Prednisone: 5 mg PO bid.

Tannock IF, et al. J Clin Oncol 1989;7:590–597.

or

  • Prednisone: 5 mg PO qid.

Fossa SD, et al. J Clin Oncol 2001;19:62–71.

2.31.2.13 Ketoconazole

  • Ketoconazole: 1,200 mg PO daily

Johnson DE, et al. Urology 1988;31:132–134.

2.31.2.14 Aminoglutethimide

  • Aminoglutethimide: 250 mg PO qid, if tolerated may increase to 500 mg PO qid

Havlin KA, et al. Cancer Treat Res 1988;39:83–96.

2.31.2.15 Sipuleucel-T

  • Sipuleucel-T: Administer contents of infusion bag IV over 60 minutes on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks for a total of 3 doses.

Kantoff PW, et al. N Engl J Med 2010;363:411–422.

2.31.2.16 Enzalutamide

  • Enzalutamide: 160 mg PO daily

Scher HI, et al. N Engl J Med 2012;367:1187–1197.

2.32 RENAL CELL CANCER

2.32.1 Adjuvant Therapy - Single-Agent Regimens

2.32.1.1 Sunitinib

  • Sunitinib: 50 mg PO daily for 4 weeks
  • Repeat cycle every 6 weeks.

Ravaud A, et al. N Engl J Med 2016;375:2246–2254.

2.32.2 Metastatic Disease - Combination Regimens

2.32.2.1 Bevacizumab + Interferon-alpha

  • Bevacizumab: 10 mg/kg IV every 2 weeks
  • Interferon alpha-2a: 9 million U SC, 3 times per week, for 1 year
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Escudier B, et al. Lancet 2007;370:2103–2111.

2.32.2.2 Interferon-alpha + IL-2

  • Interferon a-2a: 9 million U SC on days 1–4, weeks 1–4
  • Interleukin-2: 12 million U SC on days 1–4, weeks 1–4
  • Repeat cycle every 6 weeks.

Atzpodien J, et al. Semin Oncol 1993;20 (Suppl 9):22.

2.32.2.3 Lenvatinib + Everolimus

  • Lenvatinib: 18 mg/day PO daily
  • Everolimus: 5 mg/day PO daily
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Motzer RJ, et al. Lancet Oncol 2015;16:1473–1482.

2.32.2.4 Nivolumab + Ipilimumab

  • Ipilimumab: 1 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Nivolumab: 3 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for 4 cycles followed by
  • Nivolumab: 240 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 14 days until disease progression. May also administer 480 mg IV on day 1 with cycles repeated every 28 days.

Motzer RJ, et al. N Engl J Med 2018;378:1277–1290.

2.32.2.5 Bevacizumab + Everolimus

  • Bevacizumab: 10 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Everolimus: 10 mg/day PO daily
  • Repeat cycle every 14 days.

Voss MH, et al. J Clin Oncol 2016;34:3846–3853.

2.32.3 Metastatic Disease - Single-Agent Regimens

2.32.3.1 Bevacizumab

  • Bevacizumab: 10 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks.

Yang JC, et al. N Engl J Med 2003;349:427–434.

2.32.3.2 Sunitinib

  • Sunitinib: 50 mg PO daily for 4 weeks
  • Repeat cycle every 6 weeks.

Motzer RJ, et al. J Clin Oncol 2006;24:16–24.

or

  • Sunitinib: 50 mg PO daily for 2 weeks
  • Repeat cycle every 3 weeks.

Najjar YG, et al. Eur J Cancer 2014;50:1084–1089.

2.32.3.3 Sorafenib

  • Sorafenib: 400 mg PO bid
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Ratain MJ, et al. J Clin Oncol 2006;24:2505–2512.

2.32.3.4 Pazopanib

  • Pazopanib: 800 mg PO daily
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Sternberg CN, et al. J Clin Oncol 2010;28:1061–1068.

2.32.3.5 Axitinib

  • Axitinib: 5 mg PO bid; after 2 weeks may increase dose to 7 mg PO bid; after 2 weeks may increase dose to 10 mg PO bid Continue cycle every 6 weeks.

Rini Bl, et al., et al. Lancet 2011;378:1931–1939.

2.32.3.6 Temsirolimus

  • Temsirolimus: 25 mg IV weekly
  • Continue treatment disease progression.

Hudes G, et al. N Engl J Med 2007;356:2271–2281.

2.32.3.7 Everolimus

  • Everolimus: 10 mg PO daily
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Motzer RJ, et al. Lancet 2008;372:449–456.

2.32.3.8 Aldesleukin

  • Interleukin-2: 720,000 IU/kg IV every 8 hours on days 1–5 and 15–19
  • Repeat cycles in 6- to 12-week intervals up to a total of 3 cycles.

Fyfe G, et al. J Clin Oncol 1995;13:688–696.

or

  • Interleukin-2: 720,000 IU/kg IV at 8 am and 6 pm on days 1–5 and 15–19
  • Treat up to a maximum of 8 total doses on days 1–5 and repeat on days 15–19.
  • Repeat cycles in 8- to 12-week intervals.

Acquavella N, et al. J Immunother 2008;31:569–576.

2.32.3.9 Interferon-alpha

  • Interferon a-2a: 5–15 million U SC daily or 3–5 times per week Continue treatment until disease progression.

Minasian LM, et al. J Clin Oncol 1993;11:1368–1375.

2.32.3.10 Cabozantinib

  • Cabozantinib: 60 mg PO daily
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

Choueiri TK, et al. N Engl J Med 2015:373:1814–1822.

2.32.3.11 Nivolumab

  • Nivolumab: 240 mg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 2 weeks. May also administer 480 mg IV on day 1 with cycles repeated every 4 weeks.

Motzer RJ et al. Lancet Oncol 2015;16:1473–1482.

2.33 SOFT TISSUE SARCOMAS

2.33.1 Combination Regimens

2.33.1.1 AD

  • Doxorubicin: 15 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Dacarbazine: 250 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Antman K, et al. J Clin Oncol 1993;11:1276–1285.

2.33.1.2 AI

  • Doxorubicin: 20 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–3
  • Ifosfamide: 1,500 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Mesna: 225 mg/m2 IV over 1 hour before ifosfamide and at 4 and 8 hours after ifosfamide
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days. On day 5, G-CSF support should be started at 5 µg/kg/day for 10 days starting on day 5.

Worden FP, et al. J Clin Oncol 2005;23:105–112.

2.33.1.3 MAID

  • Mesna: 2,500 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–4
  • Doxorubicin: 20 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–3
  • Ifosfamide: 2,500 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–3
  • Dacarbazine: 300 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion on days 1–3
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Elias A, et al. J Clin Oncol 1989;7:1208–1216.

2.33.1.4 CYVADIC

  • Cyclophosphamide: 500 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 1.5 mg/m2 IV on day 1 (maximum, 2 mg)
  • Doxorubicin: 50 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Dacarbazine: 750 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Santoro A, et al. J Clin Oncol 1995;13:1537–1545.

2.33.1.5 Gemcitabine + Docetaxel

  • Gemcitabine: 900 mg/m2 IV over 90 minutes on days 1 and 8
  • Docetaxel: 100 mg/m2 IV on day 8
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Maki RG, et al. J Clin Oncol 2007;25:2755–2763.

2.33.1.6 Gemcitabine + Navelbine

  • Gemcitabine: 800 mg/m2 IV over 90 minutes on days 1 and 8
  • Vinorelbine: 25 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Dileo P, et al. Cancer 2007;109:1863–1869.

2.33.1.7 Doxorubicin + Olaratumab

  • Doxorubicin: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Olaratumab: 15 mg/kg IV on days 1 and 8
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Tap WD, et al. Lancet 2016;388:488–497.

2.33.1.8 CAV Alternating with IE (Ewing’s sarcoma)

  • Cyclophosphamide: 1,200 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Doxorubicin: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 2 mg IV on day 1
  • Ifosfamide: 1,800 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Etoposide: 100 mg/m2 IV on days 1–5
  • Alternate CAV with IE every 21 days for a total of 17 cycles. When the cumulative dose of doxorubicin reaches 375 mg/m2, switch to dactinomycin at 1.25 mg/m2.

Holcombe E, et al. N Engl J Med 2003;348:694–701.

2.33.2 Single-Agent Regimens

2.33.2.1 Doxorubicin

  • Doxorubicin: 75 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Santoro A, et al. J Clin Oncol 1995;13:1537–1545.

2.33.2.2 Gemcitabine

  • Gemcitabine: 1,200 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Maki RG, et al. J Clin Oncol 2007;25:2755–2763.

2.33.2.3 Ifosfamide

  • Ifosfamide: 3,000 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–3
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

van Oosterom AT, et al. Eur J Cancer 2002;38:2397–2406.

2.33.2.4 Doxorubicin Liposome

  • Doxorubicin liposome: 50 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Judson I, et al. Eur J Cancer 2001;37:870–877.

2.33.2.5 Pazopanib

  • Pazopanib: 800 mg PO daily
  • Continue treatment until disease progression.

van Der Graaf, et al. J Clin Oncol 2011;29:18S (LBA 10002).

2.33.2.6 Trabectedin

  • Trabectedin: 1.5 mg/kg IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycles every 21 days.

Demetri GD, et al. J Clin Oncol 2016;34:786–793.

2.33.2.7 Eribulin

  • Eribulin: 1.4 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Repeat cycles every 21 days.

Schoffski P, et al. Lancet 2016;387:1629–1637.

2.34 TESTICULAR CANCER

2.34.1 Adjuvant Therapy

2.34.1.1 PEB

  • Cisplatin: 20 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–5
  • Etoposide: 100 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–5
  • Bleomycin: 30 U IV on days 2, 9, and 16
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for a total of 2 cycles. Adjuvant therapy of stage II testicular cancer treated with orchiectomy and retroperitoneal lymph node dissection.

Einhorn LH, et al. J Clin Oncol 1989;7:387–391.

2.34.1.2 Carboplatin

  • Carboplatin: AUC of 7, IV on day 1
  • Administer one dose for adjuvant therapy of stage I seminoma.

Oliver RT, et al. Lancet 2005;366:293–300.

2.34.2 Metastatic Disease - Combination Regimens

2.34.2.1 BEP

  • Bleomycin: 30 U IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Etoposide: 100 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–5
  • Cisplatin: 20 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Nichols CR, et al. J Clin Oncol 1998;16:1287–1295.

2.34.2.2 EP

  • Etoposide: 100 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–5
  • Cisplatin: 20 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Bosl G, et al. J Clin Oncol 1988;6:1231–1238.

2.34.2.3 PVB

  • Cisplatin: 20 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–5
  • Vinblastine: 0.15 mg/kg IV on days 1 and 2
  • Bleomycin: 30 U IV on days 2, 9, and 16
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Einhorn LH, et al. Ann Intern Med 1977;87:293–298.

2.34.2.4 VAB-6

  • Vinblastine: 4 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Dactinomycin: 1 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Bleomycin: 30 U IV on day 1, then 20 U/m2
  • continuous infusion on days 1–3
  • Cisplatin: 20 mg/m2 IV on day 4
  • Cyclophosphamide: 600 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Vugrin D, et al. Ann Intern Med 1981;95:59–61.

2.34.2.5 VeIP (salvage regimen)

  • Vinblastine: 0.11 mg/kg IV on days 1 and 2
  • Ifosfamide: 1,200 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–5
  • Cisplatin: 20 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–5
  • Mesna: 400 mg/m2 IV, given 15 minutes before first ifosfamide dose, then 1,200 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion for 5 days
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Loehrer PJ, et al. Ann Intern Med 1988;109:540–546.

2.34.2.6 VIP (salvage regimen)

  • Etoposide (VP-16): 75 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–5
  • Ifosfamide: 1,200 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–5
  • Cisplatin: 20 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–5
  • Mesna: 400 mg/m2 IV, given 15 minutes before first ifosfamide dose, then 1,200 mg/m2/day IV continuous infusion for 5 days
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Loehrer PJ, et al. Ann Intern Med 1988;109:540–546.

2.34.2.7 TIP (salvage regimen)

  • Paclitaxel: 250 mg/m2 IV over 24 hours on day 1
  • Ifosfamide: 1,500 mg/m2/day IV on days 2–5
  • Cisplatin: 25 mg/m2/day IV on days 1–5
  • Mesna: 500 mg/m2 IV, given before ifosfamide dose, and at 4 and 8 hours after ifosfamide on days 2–5
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for a total of 4 cycles. G-CSF support at 5 µg/kg/day SC should be given on days 7–18.

Kondagunat GV, et al. J Clin Oncol 2005;23:6549–6555.

2.34.2.8 Paclitaxel + Gemcitabine

  • Paclitaxel: 100 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for a total of 6 cycles.

Einhorn LH, et al. J Clin Oncol 2007;25:513–516.

2.34.2.9 Paclitaxel + Gemcitabine + Oxaliplatin

  • Paclitaxel: 80 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Gemcitabine: 800 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 8
  • Oxaliplatin: 130 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Bokemeyer C, et al. Ann Oncol 2008;19:448–453.

2.34.3 Metastatic Disease - Single-Agent Regimens

2.34.3.1 Etoposide

  • Etoposide: 50 mg/m2 q day PO
  • Repeat cycle every 14–21 days.

Miller JC, et al. Semin Oncol 1990;17(1 Suppl 2):36–39.

2.35 THYMOMA

2.35.1 Combination Regimens

2.35.1.1 CAP

  • Cyclophosphamide: 500 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Doxorubicin: 50 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Cisplatin: 50 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Loehrer PJ, et al. J Clin Oncol 1994;12:1164–1168.

2.35.1.2 Cisplatin + Etoposide

  • Cisplatin: 60 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Etoposide: 120 mg/m2 IV on days 1–3
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Giaccone G, et al. J Clin Oncol 1996;14:814–820.

2.35.1.3 ADOC

  • Cisplatin: 50 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Doxorubicin: 40 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Vincristine: 0.6 mg/m2 IV on day 3
  • Cyclophosphamide: 700 mg/m2 IV on day 4
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days.

Fornasiero A, et al. Cancer 1991;68:30–33.

2.35.1.4 VIP

  • Etoposide: 75 mg/m2 IV on days 1–4
  • Ifosfamide: 1,200 mg/m2 IV on days 1–4
  • Cisplatin: 20 mg/m2 IV on days 1–4
  • Mesna: 240 mg/m2 IV before first ifosfamide dose, then 4 and 8 hours later on days 1–4
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for a total of 4 cycles. G-CSF support at 5 µg/kg/day should be given on days 5–15.

Loehrer PJ, et al. Cancer 2001;91:2010–2015.

2.35.1.5 Gemcitabine + Topotecan

  • Gemcitabine: 1,000 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Topotecan: 0.75–1.5 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

William WN, et al. Am J Clin Oncol 2009;32:15–19.

2.35.1.6 Carboplatin + Paclitaxel

  • Carboplatin: AUC of 6, IV on day 1
  • Paclitaxel: 225 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Lemma GL, et al. J Clin Oncol 2011;29:2060–2065.

2.36.1.1 Doxorubicin + Cisplatin

  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Shimaoka K, et al. Cancer 1985;56:2155–2160.

2.36.2.1 Doxorubicin

or

2.36.2.6 Cabozantinib (medullary carcinoma of the thyroid)

2.37 WALDENSTRÖM’S MACROGLOBULINEMIA

2.37.1 Combination Regimens

2.37.1.1 Bortezomib + Dexamethasone + Rituximab (BDR)

  • Bortezomib: 1.3 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 4, 8, and 11
  • Dexamethasone: 40 mg IV on days 1, 4, 8, and 11
  • Rituxumab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 11
  • Repeat for 4 cycles as induction therapy followed by a 12-week break and then 4 additional cycles, each given 12 weeks apart.

Treon SP, et al. J Clin Oncol 2009;27:3830–3835.

2.37.1.2 Rituximab + Dexamethasone + Cyclophosphamide

  • Rituxumab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Dexamethasone: 20 mg IV on day 1
  • Cyclophosphamide: 100 mg/m2 PO bid
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Dimopoulos MA, et al. J Clin Oncol 2007;25:3344–3349.

2.37.1.3 Carfilzomib + Dexamethasone + Rituximab (CRD)

  • Carfilzomib: 20 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 2, 8, and 9 in cycle 1 and then 36 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 2, 8, and 9 in cycles 2–6
  • Dexamethasone: 20 mg IV on days 1, 2, 8, and 9
  • Rituxumab: 375 mg/m2 IV on days 2 and 9
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days for up to 6 induction cycles, followed by an 8-week break, and then 8 additional cycles of maintenance therapy as follows:
  • Carfilzomib: 36 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 2 in cycle 1 and then 36 mg/m2 IV on days 1, 2, 8, and 9 in cycles 2–6
  • Dexamethasone: 20 mg IV on days and 1 and 2
  • Rituxumab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 2
  • Repeat cycle every 8 weeks for up to 8 cycles.

Treon SP, et al. Blood 2014;124:503–510.

2.37.1.4 Ixazomib + Dexamethasone + Rituximab (IDR)

  • Ixazomib: 4 mg/day PO on days 1, 8, and 15
  • Dexamethasone: 20 mg/day PO on days 1, 8, 15, and 22
  • Rituximab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for up to 6 cycles of induction.

Schlumberger M, et al. N Engl J Med 2015;372:621–630.

2.37.1.5 Bendamustine + Rituximab

  • Bendamustine: 90 mg/m2 IV on days 1 and 2
  • Rituxumab: 375 mg/m2 IV on day 1
  • Repeat cycle every 28 days for 4 cycles.

Castillo JJ, et al. Clin Cancer Res 2018. doi: 10.1158/1078-0432.

2.37.2 Single-Agent Regimens

2.37.2.1 Dexamethasone

  • Dexamethasone: 40 mg IV or PO on days 1–4, 9–12, and 17–20
  • Repeat cycle every 21 days.

Alexanian R, et al. Ann Intern Med 1986;105:8–11.
